# Welcome | Adaptix Framework

AdaptixC2 is ​​an extensible post-exploitation and adversarial emulation framework made for penetration testers. The Adaptix Server is written in Golang and to allow operator flexibility. The GUI Client is written in C++ QT, allowing it to be used on Linux, Windows, and MacOS operating systems.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FB6UKkj5WzVJ4Gty9dKYD%252FScreenshot_20251226_235357.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddd04b937-3f02-43b2-a7bd-4dd8c876d763&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7ee59d4&sv=2)

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/#features)

Features


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Server/Client Architecture for Multiplayer Support
    
*   Cross-platform GUI client
    
*   Fully encrypted communications
    
*   Listener and Agents as Plugin (Extender)
    
*   Task and Jobs storage
    
*   Files and Process browsers
    
*   Credentials, Targets and Screenshots Managers
    
*   Socks4 / Socks5 / Socks5 Auth support
    
*   Local and Reverse port forwarding support
    
*   BOF support
    
*   Linking Agents and Sessions Graph
    
*   Agents Health Checker
    
*   Agents KillDate and WorkingTime control
    
*   Windows/Linux/MacOs agents support
    
*   Remote Terminal / Shell
    
*   AxScript Engine
    

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/#agents)

Extension-Kit


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Official [Extension-Kit](https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/Extension-Kit)
 on GitHub

Current Extenders


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   HTTP/S Beacon Listener
    
*   SMB Beacon Listener
    
*   TCP Beacon Listener
    
*   Beacon Agent
    
*   TCP/mTLS Gopher Listener
    
*   Gopher Agent

# v0.1 -> v0.2 | Adaptix Framework

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FmNVXcQ5NX8BGBiBIK5MO%252F0.2%2520Update.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D679ca34d-dde7-47c0-a636-142395e929f5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ed0bcd0&sv=2)

**AdaptixC2**

*   AdaptixC2 adds interface support for working with Socks4 and Socks5 proxy server versions (with support for authentication, TCP/UDP, IPv4 and DNS, but not IPv6). [More...](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/tunnels-and-forwarding)
    
*   AdaptixC2 adds interface support for working with Local and Reverse TCP port forwarding. [More...](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/tunnels-and-forwarding)
    
*   AdaptixC2 improves server-client interaction;
    
*   AdaptixC2 extenders are specified in the server profile, not through a separate file. [More...](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/starting#adaptixserver)
    
*   The AdaptixServer profile now has the ability to customize the server's response to illegitimate request. [More...](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/starting#adaptixserver)
    
*   Computer field added to TasksTable in AdaptixClient;
    
*   User field added to DownloadsTable in AdaptixClient;
    
*   Changed the Logs panel of AdaptixClient;
    
*   Added the ability to connect one client to multiple servers. [More...](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/user-interface#id-1.-projects)
    
*   Light theme added to AdaptixClient;
    
*   In AdaptixClient after agent generation a window with the path to the saved file has been added;
    
*   The listener creation and agent generation dialogs now have the option to save the current configuration to a file and load it from a file;
    
*   In AdaptixClient, the Ctrl+A (Select All) keyboard shortcut now works in all tables;
    
*   In AdaptixClient, the Ctrl+L (Clear Console) keyboard shortcut now works in the agent console;
    
*   In AdaptixClient, when navigating through the command history, the command entered before navigating through the history is now cached;
    
*   AdaptixClient now has the ability to customize the interface. You can select a theme and font settings, customize the time display format in the agent console, and select fields that will not be displayed in the SessionsTable;
    
*   In AdaptixClient, the Commander class responsible for parsing arguments has been fixed;
    
*   A guide on how to create a Windows client has been added to the documentation. [More...](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation#windows-1)
    

**Agent Beacon:**

*   The Beacon agent supports Socks4 and Socks5 proxy servers (with support for authentication, TCP/UDP, IPv4 and DNS, but not IPv6);
    
*   The Beacon agent support for working with Local and Reverse TCP port forwarding;
    
*   Added BOF API: BeaconUseToken, BeaconRevertToken;
    
*   AgentExteneder now validates data received from the agent;
    
*   Fixed agent termination function. Agent correctly informs about termination;
    
*   Fixed a bug in the agent: if the server was unavailable, the agent cached the server as unavailable and did not contact it anymore.
    

**Extension-Kit:**

*   Add [Kerbeus-BOF](https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/Extension-Kit/tree/main/Kerbeus-BOF)
    
*   Add [Aliases](https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/Extension-Kit/tree/main/Aliases)
    

Last updated 10 months ago

---

# v0.4 -> v0.5 | Adaptix Framework

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.4-greater-than-v0.5#adaptixc2)

AdaptixC2


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   AdaptixClient now features a **RemoteTerminal** — a fully interactive console
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FLM5q0IM8mPs1iaXRFVNC%252FScreenshot_20250528_181244.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2c6b673c-8482-464b-bd47-744f2ae30218&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=71a65365&sv=2)

*   Tunnels can now be created from the **context menu** of the session table or the graph. It is now possible to build tunnels via AdaptixClient (**clienside**), not just through Teamserver. The tunnel mechanism has been reworked to correctly handle SSL frame formation. Information about whether a specific type of tunnel is supported by the agent is included in the tunnel configuration
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F00sBqyr0gR0UcSEtm4nG%252FScreenshot_20250528_133227.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1632792c-fa25-4769-8a92-6cb0d11123d0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=38eb333a&sv=2)

*   Command parameters can now have an empty default value
    
*   Screenshot zoom is now limited to values between x0.3 and x4.0
    
*   Columns in the TasksTable have been updated. Active tunnels are now marked as **Running** instead of **Hosted**
    
*   A [**Blogs**](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/blogs)
     section with public materials about AdaptixC2 has been added to the documentation.
    

**Fix:**

*   New methods are now used for newer versions of Qt libraries instead of deprecated ones
    
*   Indentation in tables no longer relies on QtDelegate — it is now fully implemented using QSS styles. This resolves the issue of colored spaces appearing in some tables
    
*   Fixed an issue where the client window could shrink on startup
    

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.4-greater-than-v0.5#agent-beacon)

Agent Beacon


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   Add Custom BOF API `AxAddScreenshot`
    

**Fix:**

*   Fixed the header value processing mechanism in the **BeaconHTTP** listener: [Pull Request #53](https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/AdaptixC2/pull/53)
     (by [D4rthMaulCop](https://github.com/D4rthMaulCop)
    )
    

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.4-greater-than-v0.5#agent-gopher)

Agent Gopher


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   Added Windows support
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FIpv0YM6m7prdaTjxcEG0%252FScreenshot_20250528_181011.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D80727a31-87c1-4553-b83d-5bd2a4fe868f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f44e8330&sv=2)

*   Support for multithreaded parallel SOCKS5 tunnels has been implemented.
    
*   Added **Cancel** function to the Downloads Storage
    
*   Added **Exit** option to the context menu in the session table and the graph
    
*   **FilesBrowser** now supports both file **download** and **upload**
    

**Fix:**

*   Symbolic links are now recognized, and **FilesBrowser** correctly displays them as either files or directories
    
*   File downloads were previously very slow due to a chunk size of only 10 bytes. The default chunk size for downloads is now 1 MB
    

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.4-greater-than-v0.5#extension-kit)

Extension-Kit


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New BOFs:**

*   Postex-BOF: `screenshot_bof`
    

[Previousv0.3 -> v0.4](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.3-greater-than-v0.4)

# v0.2 -> v0.3 | Adaptix Framework

If you previously used **AdaptixClient**, delete the `~/.adaptix/storage.db` file.

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.2-greater-than-v0.3#adaptixc2)

AdaptixC2


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   The session table now has agent markings: Terminated, Inactive, Unlink, No response. The operator can mark an agent as Inactive or Active, and also select the color of the entry or the entire line. The time for marking an agent as No Response is set in the session table settings. The User field now displays the access token used. Icons have appeared in the OS field.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F09Uh2sMREfzMBsGO5ucG%252FScreenshot_20250327_162107.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D394074b9-82d4-4229-946b-96684f0f4fd3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c6bb3549&sv=2)

*   Session graph added to AdaptixClient. The server implements interfaces for "internal" listeners (eg SMB listener).
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FuvESFwkQgqk4vTWOFK4H%252FScreenshot_20250327_162134.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D09824ae7-9694-422e-9409-813ff1248bb1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9afe611f&sv=2)

*   When deleting an agent from the server via the "Remove from server" menu item through the session table menu, you now need to confirm the action.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fm4HOeysZ5Q29ZHNzI03H%252FScreenshot_20250327_163010.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddf5440fb-2643-4b10-8248-3efdb7bca5e1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=99d4392b&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FjhmfYZcmkq0NlfQQi95l%252FScreenshot_20250327_163020.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D06c4f660-7ceb-4e32-9697-77838f9421f7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=345285d7&sv=2)

*   Added the User field to TasksTable. Also, all tasks now have one of the statuses: Hosted, Running, Completed. Reworked server interfaces for working with TaskData and console output, added a new task type - TYPE\_PROXY\_DATA. Extension developers received a more flexible task management mechanism.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FjIVYOFSlhVY1UhdY1U6t%252FScreenshot_20250327_162859.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd27781cd-6cc9-4b0b-bcb0-24b2d96bf239&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2fcc953d&sv=2)

*   Added search panels to SessionsTable and TaskTable. To activate the panel, use the `Ctrl+F` key combination in the table.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FNb1Rnfhet3IabmKLozwo%252FScreenshot_20250327_144957.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D14297206-fd44-49d6-9866-953f8b31e19c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b7376ff&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FvWysdSgH8yFlj2vDCqsD%252FScreenshot_20250327_145553.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D488b23a2-e76b-4588-be28-f9c469cb7a8e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5d61e22&sv=2)

*   Now, when synchronizing with the server, tasks in TasksTable will be sorted by creation time, and not by agent ID
    
*   Now when synchronizing with the server, agents in SessionsTable will be synchronized by creation time, and not by agent ID
    
*   Arguments in `help` are now displayed in formatted form.
    
*   Changed the appearance of the listener and agent creation windows (the load and save buttons have been moved to the top)
    
*   An interface for handling agent shutdown has been added to the server.
    
*   Golang packages updated from go-1.22 to go-1.23
    
*   Added docker build (by [ArchiMoebius](https://github.com/ArchiMoebius)
    )
    

**Fix:**

*   Fixed a bug in the client with packing BYTES for translation to BOF (by [ArturLukianov](https://github.com/ArturLukianov)
    )
    
*   Fixed a client bug where information was being written to the wrong field in DownloadsTable (by [uxbug](https://github.com/uxbug)
    )
    
*   Now when you close the main client window, all open windows are closed and the application exits
    
*   The main menu now works correctly in KDE panel widgets
    
*   Compliter in the agent console no longer requires additional confirmation if the text was entered manually. Duplication for commands with subcommands has been removed
    
*   On the server, situations have been fixed where the information of the last loaded module overwrote the information of previously loaded modules
    

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.2-greater-than-v0.3#agent-beacon)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   Added SMB communication channel
    
*   Added `rev2self`, `getuid`, `link`, and `unlink` commands
    
*   Sensitive strings are hidden in the agent
    
*   The service name is no longer present inside DLL, EXE, and Shellcode type agents
    
*   Added BOF API: `BeaconIsAdmin`
    
*   Added Chinese language support for coders (by [HongLuDianXue](https://github.com/HongLuDianXue)
    )
    

**Fix:**

*   Fixed memory accumulation in `ProcessDownloadTasks` (by [M1ndo](https://github.com/M1ndo)
    )
    
*   Fixed memory leaks, no more accumulation of allocated memory
    
*   The ls command now displays the correct last modification time of files
    
*   Now when creating a listener, the value of the `Port Callback` field is validated

# Getting Starting | Adaptix Framework

The Adaptix server is installed only on UNIX systems.

The following operating systems have been tested for Adaptix Client compatibility:

*   Ubuntu 22.04 / 24.04
    
*   Debian 10 / 11
    
*   Arch 2025.02.01
    
*   Kali Linux 2024.4
    
*   Windows 10 / 11
    
*   MacOS Sonoma
    

> If you have tested Adaptix on another operating system, please let me know

[Installation](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation)
[Starting](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/starting)

Last updated 6 days ago

# Starting | Adaptix Framework

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/starting#adaptixserver)

AdaptixServer


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The necessary parameters for starting the AdaptixServer can be passed via command line parameters or via a configuration file.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FBarKCF8EsdOzEtGVxfR7%252FScreenshot_20251229_201827.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D93939d56-0505-40ad-a71c-4b219ca1fb0a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bfd95275&sv=2)

The configuration file is specified in the `-profile` parameter and must contain a profile in JSON format.

**Teamserver**:

*   **port** - port for client connection
    
*   **endpoint** - URN for connecting clients
    
*   **password** - authenticator for clients
    
*   **only\_password** — If `true`, only password authentication is used for any login (Cobalt Strike mode). If `false`, authentication is used with strictly defined logins and passwords.
    
*   **cert** and **key** - SSL Certificate and Key for web server
    
*   **extender** - array of strings-paths to go-plugins
    
*   **access\_token\_live\_hours** & **refresh\_token\_live\_hours** - The validity period of the JWT token that the client receives after authorization.
    

**ServerResponse:**

*   status - web server response code in case of an illegitimate request
    
*   headers - web server HTTP Headers
    
*   page - the path to the file whose contents will be returned in the web server's response
    

**EventCallback** settings are described in [this section](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/starting/event-callback)
.

To run adaptixserver you need an SSL certificate. You can generate your own using the ssl\_gen script.

After starting AdaptixServer, a `data` directory will be created next to the server executable file. The server database file and all other files will be created in the `data` directory.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FB4aFoxrlxNX4CszxRkfI%252FScreenshot_20251229_204038.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5d329659-81d9-4aa0-bcba-bfcf796ea507&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2278d406&sv=2)

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/starting#adaptixclient)

AdaptixClient


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After the AdaptixClient is launched, a directory named `.adaptix` will be created in the user's home directory. The AdaptixClient database file will be saved in the `.adaptix` directory. In the authorization form, you must specify the profile data, user nickname (any nick), and the name of the local project.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FVMnBmVWavGvd3nKqw0cf%252FScreenshot_20251229_204213.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D60b7648a-99aa-4c7b-941f-c2a389df2339&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e3c3413e&sv=2)

After synchronizing data with the server, the main AdaptixClient window will be available.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FOKYspOwQrc2jrNGCby4E%252FScreenshot_20251229_204430.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da7a3f02d-8018-4f6d-a965-d239b52f2fd0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a25e0015&sv=2)

[PreviousInstallation](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation)
[NextEvent Callback](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/starting/event-callback)

# Event Callback | Adaptix Framework

The **EventCallback** function allows notifications about various events. At the moment, only the new agent registration event is implemented.

**new\_agent\_message** - register new agent events:

*   `%type%` - Agent type
    
*   `%id%` - Agent ID
    
*   `%user%` - Username
    
*   `%computer%` - Computer
    
*   `%domain%` - Domain name
    
*   `%pid%` - Process ID
    
*   `%internalip%` - Internal IPv4 address
    
*   `%externalip%` - External IPv4 address
    
*   `%elevated%` - `true`, if the agent has high context
    

**new\_cred\_message** - new credentials added:

*   `%username%` - Username
    
*   `%password%` - Password
    
*   `%domain%` - Realm
    
*   `%type%` - Type of secret
    
*   `%storage%` - Secrets vault
    
*   `%host%` - Computer
    

**new\_download\_message** - the file was downloaded and saved on the server:

*   `%user%` - Username
    
*   `%computer%` - Computer
    
*   `%path%` - Full filename
    
*   `%size%` - Filesize
    

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/starting/event-callback#telegram)

Telegram


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To send events to Telegram, in the `EventCallback.Telegram` configuration, you need to specify the **bot token**, as well as the **chat ID** to which the bot will send the message.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FeJakUVoqMsZStsgzgOWD%252FScreenshot_20250624_133134.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da1ecdbab-92ca-4c01-82b4-d39dbb37fbd0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f39b31dc&sv=2)

### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/starting/event-callback#create-bot)

Create BOT

1.  Go to the official [@BotFather](https://t.me/BotFather)
     bot in Telegram and create your own bot. The **API token** will be shown for the created bot.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FP3iEWjeo6l6U7r0y6OiY%252FScreenshot_20250624_213827.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0314e25f-483a-41f4-976c-ccd53ade937c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f19565e8&sv=2)

1.  Go to the created bot, activate the chat and send it any test message.
    
2.  Make a request to the Telegram API, specifying your token. The response will contain your test message and chat ID (which you will need to specify in the config)
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FJ3rpG3DflsAeVvuODNFC%252FScreenshot_20250624_214513.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D16a00210-0a88-4747-8b74-47741be47a62&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fda147df&sv=2)

If you want the bot to write to a group: add the bot to the group, assign the administrator role and write a test message to the group. Getting the chat ID is the same as for the user account.

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/starting/event-callback#webhooks)

WebHooks


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To send events to any web server, such as `ntfy.sh`, `Slack`, or `Teams`, you must specify the URL, HTTP method, request headers, and format of the data being sent in the `EventCallback.Webhooks` configuration.

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/starting/event-callback#slack)

Slack


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can use Slack WebHook to send notifications to Slack.

[PreviousStarting](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/starting)
[NextUser Interface](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/user-interface)

Last updated 2 days ago

*   [Create BOT](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/starting/event-callback#create-bot)
    
*   [WebHooks](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/starting/event-callback#webhooks)
    
*   [Slack](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/starting/event-callback#slack)

        "Telegram": {
          "token": "number:token",
          "chats_id": ["id1","id2",...]
        }

# v0.9 -> v0.10 | Adaptix Framework

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.9-greater-than-v0.10#adaptixc2)

AdaptixC2


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   **Sessions Table data model updated.** Eliminates small per-second UI stutters when many sessions are present.
    
*   **Tasks Manager data model updated.** Server synchronization is now orders of magnitude faster; loading, searching and filtering saved tasks complete in sub-second time.
    
*   **Credentials Manager data model updated.** Server sync and local data operations (read/filter) are dramatically faster.
    
*   **Targets Manager data model updated.** Synchronization and data handling significantly accelerated.
    
*   **Last column behavior changed:** if an agent has not checked in for more than 24 hours, the **Last** column shows the timestamp of the agent’s last check-in.
    
*   **Non-blocking server API calls:** API requests no longer block the main UI thread (by [newBBnew](https://github.com/newBBnew)
    )
    
*   **Cloudflare Tunnels support** added (by [newBBnew](https://github.com/newBBnew)
    )
    
*   **TLS 1.2–1.3** support added (by [newBBnew](https://github.com/newBBnew)
    )
    
*   **Client–server log sync optimized** using batch processing to improve throughput and reduce overhead (by [lsr00ter](https://github.com/lsr00ter)
    )
    

**Fix:**

*   **Tunnel handling fix:** a regression in the previous release broke task processing, which caused tunnels via linked agents to fail and made tunnels through external listeners unstable. This is now fixed.
    

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.9-greater-than-v0.10#beacon)

Beacon


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   Service messages during BOF execution are no longer spammed; the console now logs only BOF start/end events and error messages.
    

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.9-greater-than-v0.10#extension-kit)

Extension-Kit


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   `smartscan` added to SAR-BOF (by [newBBnew](https://github.com/newBBnew)
    )

    )
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fd2xFherdVlVtCAwwSpJr%252FScreenshot_20251029_221035.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbc112d8f-7510-4ec3-879d-6ff07eb90954&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ea20cf0&sv=2)

    )
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FfHApVwYsEsBkdXlLAQTT%252FScreenshot_20251029_222319.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddb0c2b0c-fbed-4eaa-ba9d-2abf5f2aa15e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8e2e0d4c&sv=2)

*   `badtakeover` added to AD-BOF
    
*   `cookie-monster` decryptor updated
    

**Fix:**

*   `poolparty`: fixed ALPC port name randomization to prevent beacon crashes with certain injection techniques (by [jacopoaugelli](https://github.com/jacopoaugelli)
    )
    
*   `ldapsearch`: LDAP signing/sealing implementation fixed.
    
*   `ldapsearch`**:** use DC hostname instead of IP for LDAP connections.
    
*   `cacls`**:** fixed out-of-bounds error.
    
*   `token make`**:** added support for multi-language usernames.

# v0.6 -> v0.7 | Adaptix Framework

Extension-Kit extensions need to be reinstalled

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.6-greater-than-v0.7#adaptixc2)

AdaptixC2


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   **Added Credential Manager**
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FID2mES4X6UgMzL9ONbkS%252FScreenshot_20250728_181635.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D61057243-e551-4475-b1b4-8aa734803ca3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a75449a4&sv=2)

*   Implemented the **AxScript scripting engine**. Added **AxScript Console** for testing AX scripts and displaying error information from user scripts.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FzMyDGyMYJNLQR6HXnY7N%252FScreenshot_20250728_185414.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D17a21b0b-55b8-4391-92dd-87f1d3f76cba&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b5769b70&sv=2)

*   The **menu in the Sessions table and Sessions graph** is now generated using AxScript. The **FileBrowser menu** is now generated using AxScript. The **DownloadsManager menu** is now generated using AxScript.
    
*   Registration of **'listener'** and **'agent'** extenders is now done through AxScript. The extender model has been significantly simplified.
    
*   It is now possible to set the **127.0.0.1** address for the Teamserver.
    
*   Help output in the client is now formatted.
    

**Fix:**

*   Fixed multithreading issues when working with tunnels.
    
*   Dockerfile updated to the required Go version.
    

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.6-greater-than-v0.7#agent-beacon)

Agent Beacon


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   Added detection of **Windows Server 2025** (by [Xre0uS](https://github.com/Xre0uS)
    ).
    
*   Added additional validation for data received from the server (by [Xre0uS](https://github.com/Xre0uS)
    ).
    
*   Implemented Beacon DLL execution via **rundll32** (by [**0xShkk**](https://github.com/0xShkk)
    ).
    
*   Rewritten the **BOF loader** implementation.
    
*   The agent no longer determines the **impersonation token**.
    
*   Added **Execute** and **Remove** menu items in FileBrowser.
    

**Fix:**

*   Fixed a potential agent hang during connection failure (by [Xre0uS](https://github.com/Xre0uS)
    ).
    
*   Listener: fixed **X-Forwarded-For** header check function (by [Xre0uS](https://github.com/Xre0uS)
    ).
    
*   Fixed **BeaconFormatAlloc** function, which could cause Beacon to crash (by [_undefo_](https://github.com/undefo)
    ).
    
*   The `ps run` command now correctly passes arguments to the application.
    

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.6-greater-than-v0.7#agent-gopher)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    ).

# Remote Terminal / Shell | Adaptix Framework

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/agent-browsers/remote-terminal-shell#remote-terminal)

Remote Terminal


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The **Remote Terminal** allows you to launch an application or command shell in fully interactive mode. For each operating system, you can either select an appropriate shell from a predefined list or specify one manually.

Linux

Windows

MacOS

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FJCMXEJM4cjCekf3Ia88d%252FScreenshot_20250528_175638.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D00bb7aa8-b67e-474a-9397-cabfcebb461d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=59e7652d&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FTWSVQwZXrp9NUbATBtpQ%252FScreenshot_20250528_181244.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcf79f40d-493b-477f-a5d0-e5787e58cd7a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5797ae0e&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FQ6LWTClCAK54095piEtv%252FScreenshot_20250528_175324.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1f35365b-31a8-4ddf-b702-1e6de0242079&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4493e87d&sv=2)

Each tab allows you to run multiple terminals in one session.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fo64OEfMJDml4Nq5Sc3EK%252FScreenshot_20251229_220225.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3b1999ae-ff17-462e-9ff3-9e8e70105be4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8abb1253&sv=2)

To start the terminal, click the ![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FTxlokXLaxiMh5nEDq1KC%252FScreenshot_20250528_183641.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbaaf102b-7333-44bd-a78a-8ffeb70c558c&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e8212f52&sv=2) button; to stop it, click the ![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FUDZ2SlrbnIcu0ZweDn8G%252FScreenshot_20250528_183657.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D13ce53b1-c09a-4f5c-a3da-642fa72df855&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=93b3d2a3&sv=2) button. The terminal includes support for **copy**, **paste**, **clear**, **find** and change console buffer size functions. By default, the console buffer only stores 10,000 lines.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FlS5TxUtxHPXiWeTenoAu%252FScreenshot_20251229_220325.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daa34117c-1ee1-42df-89b9-2aa1e00da86e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dd757234&sv=2)

**Save task to Task Manager** allows you to save the selected command and text in the manager.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FJsiyUfcf8R8YuyStMiB1%252FScreenshot_20251229_220506.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D989ba3c3-a263-4619-9e6d-d891a9782e74&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=de2c7c65&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FXOHJbyrgnR3KQYc7argv%252FScreenshot_20251229_220531.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5a5d9e14-79c2-4aec-96c3-78541ceed6c6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3f043d7f&sv=2)

You can specify a corresponding **keytab** for the terminal.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F7tiEYujE2ikmIM5D4IpK%252FScreenshot_20250528_183907.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0d406ce7-eedd-474b-9333-19f9aab520c4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=208207fb&sv=2)

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/agent-browsers/remote-terminal-shell#remote-shell)

Remote Shell


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Remote Shell feature allows you to run applications or command shells in pseudo shell mode. For each operating system, you can either select the appropriate shell from a predefined list or specify it manually.

Some shells, such as cmd.exe in echo mode, can duplicate input and output. To eliminate this duplication, use **smart mode**.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FtUwKjJvXemqTyUmd2Cyx%252FScreenshot_20251229_223421.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc25fc712-b5e1-44b5-bfd4-ba96c3f4eaa6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=636e14dc&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FJUYvEnZ2UvTWu7bJk727%252FScreenshot_20251229_223401.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D57392be4-5675-4a2f-b318-c96ffe94a362&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=43ce6ed4&sv=2)

[PreviousProcess Browser](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/agent-browsers/process-browser)
[NextData management](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/data-management)

# Installation | Adaptix Framework

The [source code](https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/AdaptixC2)
 of AdaptixС2 is available on github. The `main` branch is a stable version and does not contain the latest changes.

Copy

    git clone https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/AdaptixC2.git
    cd AdaptixC2

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation#preinstall)

Preinstall


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To build extenders you need updated Mingw. Advice on building server and extenders (**tested**): using Ubuntu 24, Debian 12, or Dockerfile.

For Linux, you can use a specially prepared script that will install and configure the necessary packages for both the server and client parts.[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation#for-linux-you-can-use-a-specially-prepared-script-that-will-install-and-configure-the-necessary-pack)

[pre\_install\_linux\_all.sh](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Adaptix-Framework/AdaptixC2/refs/heads/main/pre_install_linux_all.sh)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F73hLkX7874aTss7jqiOv%252FScreenshot_20251230_174450.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4a3e60c2-bd38-497a-a8af-1c0a6de79c47&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=603a207c&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FdI5lYBqGTLcNVOHoQDTD%252FScreenshot_20251230_175836.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3798d7dd-a995-41c0-8a4b-f8e58ee42c71&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=adf0d8a&sv=2)

To build Server and Extenders, you need to install additional dependencies. Please note that _golang 1.25.4_ is required to compile and run AdaptixServer (and special [patched golang](https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/go-win7)
 for win7 gopher agent).

Linux Debian

Linux Arch

Copy

    sudo apt install mingw-w64 make gcc g++ g++-mingw-w64
    
    wget https://go.dev/dl/go1.25.4.linux-amd64.tar.gz -O /tmp/go1.25.4.linux-amd64.tar.gz
    sudo rm -rf /usr/local/go /usr/local/bin/go
    sudo tar -C /usr/local -xzf /tmp/go1.25.4.linux-amd64.tar.gz
    sudo ln -s /usr/local/go/bin/go /usr/local/bin/go
    
    # for windows 7 support by gopher agent
    git clone https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/go-win7 /tmp/go-win7
    sudo mv /tmp/go-win7 /usr/lib/

Copy

    sudo pacman -S --needed mingw-w64 make
    
    wget https://go.dev/dl/go1.25.4.linux-amd64.tar.gz -O /tmp/go1.25.4.linux-amd64.tar.gz
    sudo rm -rf /usr/local/go /usr/local/bin/go
    sudo tar -C /usr/local -xzf /tmp/go1.25.4.linux-amd64.tar.gz
    sudo ln -s /usr/local/go/bin/go /usr/local/bin/go
    
    # for windows 7 support by gopher agent
    git clone https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/go-win7 /tmp/go-win7
    sudo mv /tmp/go-win7 /usr/lib/

To build Client, you need to install additional dependencies

Linux Debian

Linux Arch

MacOS

Windows

Need [https://doc.qt.io/qt-6/qt-online-installation.html](https://doc.qt.io/qt-6/qt-online-installation.html)

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation#makefile)

Makefile


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Server


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

AdaptixServer and Extenders (goplugins) must be built **with the same version of the golang** package.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F0gMlauK6viAZlXKwLcR7%252FScreenshot_20251127_005035.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da6c6e954-763f-4c89-a706-a273da77044f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c37725d5&sv=2)

All compiled files will be located in the dist directory.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FAMFZtrgFlrJ5dfdsrPEC%252FScreenshot_20251127_005109.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D304eaf5e-2cce-4f5d-a8d1-dbc0a879b4a8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8641d80e&sv=2)

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation#client)

Client


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation#linux-macos)

Linux / MacOS

The AdaptixClient is compiled from the cmake configuration.

For fast builds in multithreaded mode, use `make client-fast`.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F31ByKHnx8M91LAv9abOJ%252FScreenshot_20250427_113336.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da344491b-8fbc-4c98-8636-a2795bee04c4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e6f03d3f&sv=2)

AdaptixClient file will be located in the dist directory.

### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation#windows-1)

Windows

Download QT online installer from the official website: [https://www.qt.io/download-qt-installer-oss](https://www.qt.io/download-qt-installer-oss)
.

After launching the installer, on the package download page, check the boxes as shown in the screenshot below.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fq0N61ryYanP7teJGIXnX%252FScreenshot_20250722_230232.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D80b2182d-de1f-4610-89dc-e20dc57bfa98&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9add3a41&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FdhQRygtuirbXiNgVaRk7%252FScreenshot_20250722_230239.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc4ed7a00-f301-46df-97f6-8b9ce92832be&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5e885ba9&sv=2)

In QT Creator, select **Open Project,** select the **CMakeLists.txt** file and click on **Configure Project**.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F9pd4dj5rJFaMoM8D0W5u%252FScreenshot_20250927_203032.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D20157bfb-8013-4a99-8efa-3410fd6f908f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=223941e1&sv=2)

After Configuration the project, change the build type to **Release** and build the project.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F7DbjKdsAiNd89wq3fdg8%252FScreenshot_20250927_203203.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9cbca782-c1e2-4b03-ba29-47d258cb3d0f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=80d8df54&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F7FLkdU9O4aiOz2jFCk54%252FScreenshot_20250927_203218.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9cb14c80-a9d6-4738-abb1-71c5260a0b4b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=78452953&sv=2)

Create a directory for the client where all dependencies will be copied. Move the AdapticClient.exe executable to this directory, open cmd.exe and run **windeployqt.exe.**

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FM8Zdm1O8KrOuLC1y18Nz%252F03.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddda3c266-8f4d-444d-8e00-6a12736facd4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9da3663c&sv=2)

The directory with the application and dependencies can be transferred to any computer.

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation#docker-compose)

Docker Compose


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Profile

Description

Command

`build-server`

Build server only

`docker compose --profile build-server up`

`build-extenders`

Build extenders only

`docker compose --profile build-extenders up`

`build-server-ext`

Build server and extenders together

`docker compose --profile build-server-ext up`

`runtime`

Server runtime container

`docker compose --profile runtime up -d`

Added Docker cleanup targets for better build artifact management:

*   `docker-clean`: Remove Docker containers and images (builders only)
    
    *   Removes containers and images for `build-server`, `build-extenders`, and `build-server-ext` profiles
        
    *   Preserves runtime container
        
    
*   `docker-clean-all`: Remove all Docker artifacts (containers, images, volumes, networks)
    
    *   Removes all build profiles including runtime
        
    *   Cleans build output directories (`AdaptixServer/server-dist`)
        
    *   Complete cleanup for fresh rebuilds

Copy

    sudo apt install gcc g++ build-essential make cmake mingw-w64 g++-mingw-w64 libssl-dev qt6-base-dev qt6-base-private-dev libxkbcommon-dev qt6-websockets-dev qt6-declarative-dev

Copy

    sudo pacman -S --needed make cmake openssl libxkbcommon qt6-base qt6-websockets qt6-declarative

Copy

    # https://brew.sh/
    brew install make cmake openssl qt@6

Copy

    make server-ext

Copy

    make client

# v0.5 -> v0.6 | Adaptix Framework

Go version has been updated from 1.23.1 to 1.24.4, so **a full installation** [**following the guide**](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation#preinstall)
 **is required**.

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.5-greater-than-v0.6#adaptixc2)

AdaptixC2


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   **Agent Console – Path Autocompletion & File Selection Dialog.** Local file path autocompletion is now available in the agent console via the `Tab` key. Pressing `Ctrl+Tab` opens a **file selection dialog** for browsing the file system.
    
*   **Context Menu Enhancements (Agent Console & Logs Panel).** A context menu has been added to both the agent console and the Logs panel, allowing you to configure _AutoScroll_, _NoWrap_, and change the _console buffer size_ (limiting the number of lines). Default values for AutoScroll, NoWrap, and buffer size can be configured in Main Settings.
    
*   Search functionality (`Ctrl+F`) has been added to the agent console and the Logs panel.
    
*   Command history in the agent console is now restored upon synchronization with the server, even after client reconnection. Full history is available through the “Show History” context menu. Double-clicking a command in Show History inserts it into the input field.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FmkXmVRntMsnYHXx47vEg%252FScreenshot_20250624_002427.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Debb605d4-039a-41d0-a980-733173b37fc4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=586fb52a&sv=2)

*   In **RemoteTerminal**, buffer size (line count) can now be configured via the context menu. The default value can be set in Main Settings.
    
*   **EventCallback** to Telegram BOT. [More...](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/starting/event-callback)
    
*   **New UI Theme and Font Support**. A new _Dracula_ theme has been added to AdaptixClient. It can be selected in client settings. Font support for _DejaVu Sans Mono_ and _Hack_ has been extended. New fonts _Space Mono_ and _Anonymous Pro_ have been added.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FFVk2xQleAQU3cbypmkoH%252FScreenshot_20250624_002057.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da0568e8f-9793-4f38-bf6e-b56f352450f5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a90d1c99&sv=2)

*   The columns _Domain_, _Computer_, and _User_ in SessionsTable can now be resized manually.
    
*   **Enhanced Session Table Menu.** The session table menu has been redesigned. It is now possible to execute a command on multiple agents via the **'Agent' → 'Execute command'** menu. Console content can be permanently deleted via **'Agent' → 'Remove console data'**, while all tasks remain in TasksManager.
    
*   An additional graph version has been added (by [mil4ne](https://github.com/mil4ne)
    ). You can select which version to use in client settings.
    

Version 1

Verison 2

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fqon6CsftqH2HhGo8ZsH6%252FScreenshot_20250624_000616.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D413e973a-c30f-437d-951c-019aadc8551c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=83375a08&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FEP1Ej9opE50ur4sfi1oJ%252FScreenshot_20250624_000636.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd6cb25e2-6045-4928-8373-1e32eba188d8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c8b9414c&sv=2)

*   All settings are now applied in real time and no longer require a client restart.
    
*   **One-Time Password (OTP) Token System**. An OTP token system has been added for one-time access to objects. The endpoint `/otp/get` accepts the object type and its identifier (e.g. type: download, id: FileId). With the received token, you can access the `/download/sync/otp` endpoint and download a file once without authentication on the team server. Tasks larger than 5 MB are now uploaded as files using OTP. [More...](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/data-management/downloads-manager)
    
*   Synchronization of large files from DownloadsTable has been implemented. Files are uploaded through the client in a separate thread. A new window shows synchronization status and speed. You can also obtain an OTP and download the file via Curl or Wget. [More...](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/data-management/downloads-manager)
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FzhMZODwqDae5SC0ApjWw%252FScreenshot_20250624_000922.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D28a54e42-eb7f-442c-9abe-ec224ac815e6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8ef7c75e&sv=2)

*   When restoring agents from the database, the client log now shows the date and time the agent was created.
    
*   The C2 endpoint may now contain the "." character.
    
*   Project structure has been refactored. Client build time has been reduced by approximately 50%.
    
*   Server has been updated from Go 1.23.1 to Go 1.24.4.
    

**Fix:**

*   Fixed an [issue](https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/AdaptixC2/issues/82)
     with incorrect task data validation. The client would terminate when executing a sequence of commands involving `file upload` and Beacon `agent termination`.
    
*   Fixed an issue with caching unsynchronized tasks. These tasks are no longer stored in server memory unless they are JOBs.
    
*   When copying Cmdline from TasksBrowser, an incorrect column value was copied. Now dynamic column indices are used.
    
*   Fixed color inconsistencies in the agent console when pasting previously copied data. The agent console no longer uses HTML for text formatting.
    
*   Fixed padding in UI styles. Buttons and input fields now have equal height.
    

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.5-greater-than-v0.6#agent-beacon)

Agent Beacon


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   In the BeaconSMB listener, pipe names can now contain "." characters.
    
*   The `ps list` command now displays processes as a tree structure.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FpWFpGOZwzsgJDfHK1YEQ%252FScreenshot_20250624_002639.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6daf2674-5655-444c-a10a-c0f812f4adfe&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=572b34a5&sv=2)

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.5-greater-than-v0.6#agent-gopher)

Agent Gopher


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   The `shell` and `run` commands now support various encodings.
    
*   Executing `shell` and `run` commands no longer opens a visible console window (by [yinsel](https://github.com/yinsel)
    )
    
*   Added support for legacy Windows systems, including Windows 7 and Windows Server 2003 (by [yinsel](https://github.com/yinsel)
    ).
    

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.5-greater-than-v0.6#extension-kit)

Extension-Kit


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New BOFs:**

*   Postex-BOF: `firewallrule add` (by [B1oodyPhoenix](https://github.com/B1oodyPhoenix)
    )
    
*   Process-BOF: `process conn` (by [B1oodyPhoenix](https://github.com/B1oodyPhoenix)
    )
    
*   Creds-BOF: `hashdump` (by [ArturLukianov](https://github.com/ArturLukianov)
    )

# v0.8 -> v0.9 | Adaptix Framework

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.8-greater-than-v0.9#adaptixc2)

AdaptixC2


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   Rewrote the client core — the client now uses a dock-based structure.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F1B6aWVVxDmiuEB3XrMrQ%252FScreenshot_20250927_213254.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dab0f5423-8d11-4bb3-97bd-c4eff8e478c1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7ebff42c&sv=2)

*   AxScript new functions: [agent\_hide](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction#agent_hide)
    , [agent\_remove](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction#agent_remove)
    , [hash](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction#hash)
    , [random\_string](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction#random_string)
    , [random\_int](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction#random_int)
    .
    
*   Added new API `POST /agent/task/save` to save a task to the Tasks Manager.
    
*   Remote Terminal: you can now select a command response and save it to the Tasks Manager.
    
*   After server sync, files downloaded in DownloadsManager are now sorted by date.
    
*   Added a multithreaded client build.
    
*   Server web-APIs [published](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/server-web-api)
    .
    
*   Authentication: users can now authenticate to the server either with a master password or with credentials hard-coded in the profile. (by [exil-security](https://github.com/exil-security)
    )
    
*   Optimised Exist DB functions — the Exist functions now query IDs directly instead of iterating through all rows. (by [Xre0uS](https://github.com/Xre0uS)
    )
    
*   Added a confirmation dialog when deleting a listener. (by [newBBnew](https://github.com/newBBnew)
    )
    
*   In addition to Telegram notifications, added the ability to notify any web service (for example ntfy.sh, Slack, or Microsoft Teams). (by [mdube99](https://github.com/mdube99)
    )
    

**Fix:**

*   Fixed a bug where the client login configuration would not update. (by [newBBnew](https://github.com/newBBnew)
    )
    
*   Fixed a bug where the agent command configuration would not update when the user re-logged in. (by [newBBnew](https://github.com/newBBnew)
    )
    

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.8-greater-than-v0.9#beacon)

Beacon


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   Added BOF API `AxDownloadMemory(char* filename, char* data, int len);`
    

**Fix:**

*   Fixed bug in `getuid` command (by [overflow0verture](https://github.com/overflow0verture)
    )
    
*   Encryption keys for HTTP/SMB/TCP listeners can now be set at listener creation. (by [newBBnew](https://github.com/newBBnew)
    )
    

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.8-greater-than-v0.9#gopher)

Gopher


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Fix:**

*   Added BOF API `AxAddScreenshot(char* note, char* data, int len);`
    
*   Added BOF API `AxDownloadMemory(char* filename, char* data, int len);`
    
*   Encryption keys for listeners can now be set at listener creation. (by [newBBnew](https://github.com/newBBnew)
    )
    

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.8-greater-than-v0.9#extension-kit)

Extension-Kit


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   `psexec`: now more configurable.
    
*   `inject-poolparty`: eight injection techniques for processes. (by [jacopoaugelli](https://github.com/jacopoaugelli)
    )
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FN782JbjP7YForB1sHIP7%252FScreenshot_20250927_220630.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D685d0839-a90b-4f7b-bd10-727b42a39017&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1129a906&sv=2)

*   `nanodump`: now produces a dump file from process memory
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FyvnE4ChPbrhjWa7I4vxx%252FScreenshot_20250927_215358.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db0722a95-24cb-4e10-a2bf-cf78586eca43&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e70d0c63&sv=2)

*   `cookie-monster`: retrieves Chrome encryption key and downloads files from the Chrome process memory
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FQRpVvJf3Ochh1CcuCrBQ%252FScreenshot_20250927_215748.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D139dc8e3-9b9a-4851-901e-4fd6b8c08028&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cdbb46a7&sv=2)

*   `get-netntlm`: BOF implementation of Internal-Monologue.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F3vCAx7cRQvPUuX3600ZJ%252FScreenshot_20250927_215922.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D546525b2-19af-4aa1-88de-ecd1651cbd0b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ddd87b29&sv=2)

*   `invoke-winrm`: execute commands via WinRM.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FQlzmLpE2H2BE2jBlWcG9%252FScreenshot_20250927_221914.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De2358f63-5890-45d0-b47a-4dc73c2ca962&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3508ef5e&sv=2)

# Process Browser | Adaptix Framework

The Process Browser displays information about processes. When the Process Browser is launched, **no requests are made to the server**. To send a request to the server, you must click the Refresh button ![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FwaspTq83XEWIT06VALQu%252F40.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3343f776-f79c-40a7-beea-dd4db5448f1c&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1e42f943&sv=2).

The Process Browser on the left displays the processes in a tree view. The table on the right displays detailed information about the processes. The current process running the agent is displayed in red.

Windows

Unix

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FwaeMfB6yipzBwiLdpcJd%252F41.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0d8549cc-4cee-4892-adf3-dfd09d57be26&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a812f9c0&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F3DLZZPemqW27QULUxDdY%252FScreenshot_20250427_123332.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df02f6753-3c37-434a-8c56-a28706005dc6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d011aac3&sv=2)

The "Wait" status indicates that the request is currently being processed. The "Ok" status displays the date and time of the response.

Wait

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FNgRJ5ZJGq7rogodRhkME%252F42.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5337b2cb-95ca-43f8-b176-8fdf8606585a&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5d1bc11c&sv=2)

Ok

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fm4fnP0DGgBKM80XUVzBF%252F43.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da552190a-0f5a-444a-8e58-5da7129e26d0&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2c1a6228&sv=2)

File Browser allows you to filter processes by a substring from any column.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FJiPsD4hcekv79NbB7ykN%252F44.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D000f9dc3-8a6b-4434-ab13-7ccba6e89264&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9d082616&sv=2)

From the context menu of the process table you can copy the PID of the selected process.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FZMztJ1rtAwAHqM0cGJtZ%252F45.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6a9d6bba-14c7-4bbe-a264-a757077ac699&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ff0e9dae&sv=2)

[NextRemote Terminal / Shell](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/agent-browsers/remote-terminal-shell)

# Downloads Manager | Adaptix Framework

The Downloads Tab displays all current or completed downloads.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FjsCu2HeSe8EhWLG0UkN3%252F52.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D07070220-6b6e-4d7a-b63b-018b2ce66112&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f67f7bf4&sv=2)

The context menu provides options to cancel the download, as well as stop and resume the download.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FtQx7xgyIr2UAahiYhSXu%252F53.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daed1de7b-3ee0-4def-ab95-5b003fe0473e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8eeb84b0&sv=2)

The downloaded files are stored on AdaptixServer. To copy a file from the server to the client system, select it and click "Sync file to client". Adaptix will then download the selected files to the folder on your system that you selected in the dialog box.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FOweMGJb9UjfGuV5V9uGO%252F54.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De04fda7a-0a98-483d-9a47-e924d2ef1e44&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=311fd2ac&sv=2)

[PreviousTasks manager](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/data-management/tasks-manager)
[NextTargets Manager](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/data-management/targets-manager)

Last updated 11 months ago

# v0.10 -> v0.11 | Adaptix Framework

Go version has been updated from 1.24.4 to 1.25.4, so **a full installation** [**following the guide**](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation#preinstall)
 **is required**.

Contributed to this update: [shashinma](https://github.com/shashinma)
, [cr0eax](https://github.com/cr0eax)
, [Xre0uS](https://github.com/Xre0uS)
, [M1ndo](https://github.com/M1ndo)
, [ArturLukianov](https://github.com/ArturLukianov)
, [entropy-z](https://github.com/entropy-z)

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.10-greater-than-v0.11#adaptixc2)

AdaptixC2


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   Golang has been updated from version 1.24.4 to 1.25.4. The new version will use the new experimental `encoding/json/v2` package and the new experimental `greenteagc` garbage collector.
    
*   Synchronization of extension package versions and the framework itself is now controlled by a single `go work` statement.
    
*   The synchronization mechanism has been optimized. The entire client interface is now blocked during synchronization.
    
*   The `GenerateUI` function in axscript now also returns the `ui_height` and `ui_width` properties, which adjust the window for creating listeners or agents.
    
*   Client UI: Add dynamic title bar styling based on theme (by [shashinma](https://github.com/shashinma)
    )
    
*   Added building server and extenders in [docker compose](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation#docker-compose)
     (by [shashinma](https://github.com/shashinma)
    )
    

**Fix:**

*   Fixed errors with interrupted upload and synchronization of large files.
    
*   Fixed an issue where the sync progress bar would not appear when reconnecting to the server.
    

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.10-greater-than-v0.11#beacon)

Beacon


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   Classes that store this during initialization will get pointer to temporary memory (on stack) because of current construction method. Code changed to use new/delete with overridden operator new/operator delete for each of beacon class. (by [cr0eax](https://github.com/cr0eax)
    )
    

**Fix**:

*   Problem in `BeaconFormatPrintf`/`BeaconPrintf` because `vsnprintf` returns -1 on error which is later used as size leading to crash (by [cr0eax](https://github.com/cr0eax)
    )
    
*   Problem in `BeaconAddValue` and family. It stores `Char*` as raw pointer inside `Map<CHAR*, LPVOID> Values;` Changed to store actual key value (by [cr0eax](https://github.com/cr0eax)
    )
    
*   Ntdll `RtlRandomEx`, `RtlGetVersion` `__stdcall` for x86 (crash on shifted stack) (by [cr0eax](https://github.com/cr0eax)
    )
    

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.10-greater-than-v0.11#gopher)

Gopher


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   Golang has been updated from version 1.24.4 to 1.25.4.
    

**Fix:**

*   Fixed an issue where the agent would not have a delay between reconnections.
    
*   The `cat` command now has a 10 KB limit.
    

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.10-greater-than-v0.11#extension-kit)

Extension-Kit


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   AD-BOF: Added `readlaps` BOF (by [Xre0uS](https://github.com/Xre0uS)
    )
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FxBwi9NiDw7jFHZn3rzmB%252FScreenshot_20251116_104251.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0d509ed4-c4f8-4a58-b17d-3010ff342139&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=16636073&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F7pGnyG25QLSDyUo1mu4R%252FScreenshot_20251116_104303.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D22093f6f-72bf-43dc-95dc-5a5ad4547194&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3501a380&sv=2)

*   Postex-BOF: adde `SauronEye-BOF` (by [shashinma](https://github.com/shashinma)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fqb43uLyETMAwulAVpI5K%252FScreenshot_20251124_190519.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D436290bc-042b-4973-a792-969496299cb0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ee3cdf6&sv=2)

    )
