    )
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FLrrIJkknvFToEqagBNhN%252FScreenshot_20251125_230852.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D659db62c-aa51-4926-91d8-b6c0bc031fa0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=38a5245b&sv=2)

*   Injection-BOF: Added `inject-32to64` BOF (by [Xre0uS](https://github.com/Xre0uS)
    )
    
*   LateralMovement-BOF: added `jump scshell` BOF (by [Xre0uS](https://github.com/Xre0uS)
    )
    
*   LateralMovement-BOF: added `invoke scshell` BOF (by [Xre0uS](https://github.com/Xre0uS)
    )
    
*   Elevation-BOF: Added `potato print` BOF
    

**Fix:**

*   MSSQL-BOF: parse flags before positional arguments (by [Xre0uS](https://github.com/Xre0uS)
    )
    
*   MSSQL-BOF: fixed `mssql clr`, was missing the DLL bytes and hash (by [Xre0uS](https://github.com/Xre0uS)
    )
    
*   Kerbeus-BOF: Add `kerbeus describe` (by [Xre0uS](https://github.com/Xre0uS)
    )
    
*   In some environments `parsed_json` is not returning as a standard JS object, causing `Error: Property 'hasOwnProperty' of object TypeError: Type error is not a function`. Switched to using "property" in `parsed_json` instead of `parsed_json.hasOwnProperty("property")` (by [Xre0uS](https://github.com/Xre0uS)
    )
    

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.10-greater-than-v0.11#templates-extender)

templates-extender


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Golang has been updated from version 1.24.4 to 1.25.4
    

### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v0.10-greater-than-v0.11#new-community-extenders)

New community extenders

*   [PaperShell](https://github.com/ArturLukianov/PaperShell)
     (by [ArturLukianov](https://github.com/ArturLukianov)
    ) - Simple Powershell agent for Adaptix C2. + HTTP Listener
    
*   [Kharon](https://github.com/entropy-z/Kharon-Agent)
     (by [entropy-z](https://github.com/entropy-z)
    ) - Fully PIC agent that operates without a reflective loader and includes evasion features such as sleep obfuscation, heap obfuscation during sleep, stack spoofing with indirect syscalls, BOF API proxy for spoofed/indirect BOF API executions, and AMSI/ETW bypass. + HTTP/S Listener

# Linking Agents | Adaptix Framework

AdaptixC2 supports agent chains (linking agents). These linked agents receive their commands and send their output through the parent agent in their chain. This type of chaining is useful to control which sessions egress a network and to emulate a disciplined actor who restricts their communication paths inside of a network to something plausible.

For a linked agent, the External field will contain the parent agent ID and link name instead of the external IP address. Registered but not currently linked agents are marked as Unlink.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FmraoZhutN4PFCLXEOa0p%252FScreenshot_20251229_211625.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd8460751-69fe-4b24-a40d-21fe09b5d641&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cf8ce333&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F4UcuHLAYzlHdPXwjYMln%252FScreenshot_20251229_211531.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5a057e63-b9eb-4d08-95c2-73ca7bc7aabc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cdd7c9d5&sv=2)

# New extenders | Adaptix Framework

Templates for developing your own Extenders agents and listeners are located in [THIS](https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/templates-extender)
 repository. Since Extenders uses goplugin technology, the core framework package versions and all extenders must be the same. Go Workspace technology is used to easily manage large numbers of extenders.

All actions are performed in the `AdaptixServer` directory.

1.  Move your extenders in the `AdaptixServer/extenders` directory and add them to the workspace.
    

Copy

    go work use extenders/new_listener_extender
    go work use extenders/new_agent_extender

1.  Sync Go Workspace
    

Copy

    go work sync

1.  Build the extenders and specify the path to the `config.json` in the server profile.
    

Copy

    make extenders

* * *

Last updated 1 month ago

# Tasks manager | Adaptix Framework

A task can be of two types:

*   TASK — a fast task, executed in a single-threaded mode, delaying all other agent functions.
    
*   JOB — a task executed in the background. As a rule, such a task is executed longer in a separate thread or process. BOF can also be executed.
    
*   TUNNEL — a task indicating the start or stop of network tunnels.
    

AdaptixС2 registers and saves in the database all tasks ever completed. The task table displays the task type, the operator who started the task, the time of task execution, its status and a short answer.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fvu9QyBBmzUMWDS9Z33Me%252FScreenshot_20250224_214344.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f967d38-0a6f-4d7a-8835-05e58baaeb3d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d12b7fa9&sv=2)

The output of a specific command is displayed in the Task Output console when you select a task in the Tasks table.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FY274AqSPwxyrnI70KcjB%252F47.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6d86285a-6a4c-4d51-93b9-96ddf57eb8e4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3b3a5a8e&sv=2)

To activate the search bar, you must use the key combination `Ctrl+F` in the task table.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FygkfKzB879POlsDinORP%252FScreenshot_20251229_212104.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D389bf1c9-f90d-4e64-8273-f7e51c24d346&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=20ebb484&sv=2)

The Tasks table has the ability to filter tasks by individual agents.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FoFe469S3bmNcqKMTr1CA%252FScreenshot_20251229_212117.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da27293e2-de73-44e1-9e95-4966bdb81d4c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=afaa60e1&sv=2)

Tasks can be filtered by status. For example, you can filter only cancelled tasks or only those that are in progress (convenient for Jobs).

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FpJwuZtN8gUHH7bVRRrNf%252FScreenshot_20251229_212141.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D052f78d5-d4eb-497b-a15f-8524a843680f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5330e453&sv=2)

The Task table has the ability to filter by a substring in a command or by the result of its execution.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FxtM9Uv5k2qqijhG0rpEO%252FScreenshot_20251229_212223.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D55a90322-3307-4474-a1f5-7d4ddacc4c7f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d6d64e60&sv=2)

The context menu provides options to terminate the currently running task, as well as delete tasks from the database. In addition, you can quickly copy the task ID or console command and immediately go to the console of the selected agent.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FI6ToSqMoyz6U6S2gp779%252F51.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2caaed35-2f9f-432c-9366-031bf850fd93&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=13f425d3&sv=2)

[PreviousData management](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/data-management)
[NextDownloads Manager](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/data-management/downloads-manager)

# Beacon SMB | Adaptix Framework

"Beacon SMB" is an internal listener used to communicate with the "Beacon" agent over SMB named pipes.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F95YKiQ7KxEUMFdPqu82i%252FScreenshot_20251229_201042.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8541145f-f3ea-4b4d-bd92-f04359d1b45c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a034a02&sv=2)

# File Browser | Adaptix Framework

File Browser is an opportunity to explore the files on a compromised system. The left-hand side of the file browser is a tree which organizes the known drives and folders into one view. The right-hand side of the file browser shows the contents of the current folder.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fri5Gmw65rVtvIOv5gfch%252F25.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8d1ba232-0b19-4874-bce8-84220c78a31c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ff569264&sv=2)

When you launch the File Browser, **no request is made to the server**. If the path is empty, you can click the "Refresh" button ![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F4YdqCaD4hDCPRAqsir1J%252F26.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db9d24dab-701f-4bba-850f-9de0040b9a78&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=12c16499&sv=2), after which the contents of the working directory will be requested. Another option: specify the desired directory in the path field and click the "Go to" button ![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F6x2zTGNu0RskJV7BhPw1%252F27.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc236c80d-ca6a-4234-9127-191e004c33d2&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=21d672c9&sv=2).

Windows

Unix

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fpj2mle4HbU3ElTO4oRYw%252F28.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D206f6bb0-b495-4bbd-acf4-833c1fc75057&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3b5a4be0&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FzcXxHRAypMZqKX65vUnI%252FScreenshot_20250427_123146.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D790e0d55-a0c9-4588-b92f-dc790f8f9961&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c1161d7e&sv=2)

After each request, File Browser caches the contents of the requested directory. An open folder ![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F9PCFB2ESjKci5yOFlqLv%252F29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcaff5d49-c772-4555-b3c8-efd4d1b1044c&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9041f2b0&sv=2) (as opposed to a closed folder ![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FzJ9UMZNlqA0mAQR8gowf%252F30.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dad3084e6-cfe2-4924-a6ad-4c703d47c017&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=630992db&sv=2)) indicates that the folder's contents have been cached. You can navigate to cached folders without creating a new file listing request. Click "Refresh" to refresh the contents of the current folder. Double-clicking on a directory in the table or directory tree will cause the browser to navigate to that directory. To go up a level, click the folder button ![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Foylq2ykL1DPz7e9y1ACr%252F34.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D87daa456-a81f-4b19-a54e-ba1cf511b415&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6cc425b5&sv=2) next to the file path.

Along with the directory contents, its status is also cached. The "wait" status indicates that the request is currently being processed. The "Ok" status displays the date and time the response was cached. The "Error" status contains additional information about the cause of the error.

Wait

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FEJc1v5H5DWzP76RTCREI%252F31.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D069b054e-53e5-4531-ac7f-0c58d8c871ed&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=55c71f7f&sv=2)

Ok

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FC4PuOkTAO2zaJHI9z8V9%252F32.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8507c6d7-19bb-4e97-bef9-7a44b223f4dc&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6f16373e&sv=2)

Error

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FyRzwtfVHo43vRtroes8A%252F33.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D76435941-6522-4cc0-b395-c412e47fe33a&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d95f5855&sv=2)

To upload a file to the current directory, you can use the "Upload" button ![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fp3aahwCRl4lA0Sh8gxda%252F35.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D28b0f719-7003-4749-a683-6c99fec29211&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2091b3f2&sv=2). To download a file from the host, you can use the command from the context menu.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FotSTpeZrcKVb4OZewFQZ%252F36.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd70af61c-f8dd-40dd-ba66-6abdddad9560&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2cf74f69&sv=2)

To see which drives are available, press "Disks" button ![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fd0BuMBWpjOiY4hUiQ4Pc%252F37.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5bc2fc29-bb96-4e01-aa46-b18688f9ac0e&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8ac4e2c&sv=2).

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fu9L83ONUaD1CpFqFSnbr%252F38.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da685e5c7-d4a9-488b-a197-1522ad8b7aeb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=efc2369d&sv=2)

# Credentials Manager | Adaptix Framework

The Credentials Tab displays all stored credentials.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FtXdtuzqWadRQS8fCzrrb%252FScreenshot_20250728_181635.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D71cfc370-5b23-42ac-9802-843090558f17&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6cc2efc6&sv=2)

The context menu provides the ability to create a new item, edit or delete an existing one.

`%realm%` - will be replaced by realm from credentials

`%username%` - will be replaced by username from credentials

`%password%` - will be replaced by password from credentials

# Beacon TCP | Adaptix Framework

The "Beacon TCP" uses a TCP socket to communicate through a parent Beacon agent. This peer-to- peer communication works with Beacons on the same host and across the network.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Ff5nVv18cufTfNQHH13Ws%252FScreenshot_20251229_201048.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc4210137-9956-4f03-8b12-1aa89c4c06fe&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=687fb0f0&sv=2)

*   **Bind port —** Default TCP Beacon listen port
    
*   **Prepend data —** Prepend header to TCP Beacon messages
    
*   **Enctyption key —** Communication channel encryption key
    

[PreviousBeacon SMB](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/listeners/beacon-smb)
[NextGopher TCP](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/listeners/gopher-tcp)

Last updated 2 days ago

# Tunnels and Forwarding | Adaptix Framework

AdaptixC2 provides the ability to use several pivot options. For each of these options, you need to make sure that yours agent supports a specific feature and is in interactive mode (sleep 0). By default, the agent is not put into interactive mode.

### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/tunnels-and-forwarding#create-tunnels)

Create tunnels

Create a tunnel using the **Create Tunnel** context menu of the session table or graph if the agent supports one of the tunnel types.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F5VdviQJ77N9wsHjJ5Lu9%252FScreenshot_20250727_223330.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dde6e74b0-088d-4390-9f15-3cc70a640caa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e75e72a3&sv=2)

AdaptixC2 supports the following types of network tunnels:

*   SOCKS4
    
*   SOCKS5 (with/out Auth) TCP/UDP (IPv4, DNS, **not IPv6**)
    
*   Local TCP Port Forwarding
    
*   Reverse TCP Port Forwarding
    

Socks5

Socks4

Local port Forwarding

Reverse port Forwarding

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F00sBqyr0gR0UcSEtm4nG%252FScreenshot_20250528_133227.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1632792c-fa25-4769-8a92-6cb0d11123d0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=38eb333a&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FoABv8Y0s6moHLyi5WRtJ%252FScreenshot_20250528_133233.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8aaef832-b913-4032-a3d7-f51377705bdc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e1984f36&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FbrMqNKvY9lE8zaJLwMxK%252FScreenshot_20250528_133238.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D669d0d01-86e9-4892-abd1-88264559f9f1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4c2815c0&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FuKv7Mfx6GbvlEGazcqGl%252FScreenshot_20250528_133244.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Defd69026-a64b-4ab0-949b-f59903ea9d3b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d3b6eac2&sv=2)

AdaptixC2 allows you to build tunnels not only through the C2 teamserver (route: `-> C2 -> agent -> target`), but also through AdaptixClient.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fj7vglFRkjQUSwJ3m0YXW%252FScreenshot_20250528_133325.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D07de4f87-03a5-46d5-a21a-dd51a18fb1a5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9e10796d&sv=2)

In this case, the port is opened on the client and the traffic is directed along the path: `-> Client -> C2 -> agent -> target`.

### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/tunnels-and-forwarding#tunnel-manager)

Tunnel manager

Created tunnels are managed via the tunnel manager.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FI1tAvuvvA6imHhl4jz8l%252FScreenshot_20250225_001926.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De9befa7b-7b83-4448-bb67-51de1efff2bc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d6a3a0d7&sv=2)

The context menu of the Tunnels Table allows you to set information about the tunnel and stop the tunnel.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F2IrfdNH65KfvHiFIceFI%252FScreenshot_20250225_001938.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7afa1c9e-6c7c-4ab9-baa7-33c1934c436e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=590068f9&sv=2)

Management of tunnels running through a client is available only to the user through whose client the tunnel is running

# Gopher TCP | Adaptix Framework

"Gopher TCP" listener starts a tcp/mtls server and registers a "gopher" agent.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F2IrY86OwaVR4E00FITxS%252FScreenshot_20251229_201056.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D24bc34d0-599b-4fa7-ad9a-e48acbb4c809&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=608e766e&sv=2)

Parameter

Description

**Host & port (Bind)**

**Required.** The interface address and port to which your TCP Gopher server will bind.

**Callback addresses**

**Required.** List of address:port to which the agent will send requests. Current server rotation strategy: round-robin.

**Timeout (sec)**

The time to wait between connections in the event of a connection failure or interruption

**TCP banner**

Data that the server will send when any client connects to the port

**Error answer**

Server response if agent is not registered

**Encryption key**

Communication channel encryption key

**Use mTLS**

If set, use mTLS. Certificates and keys are not generated on the server

**How to Generate Certificates and Keys for mTLS**

[PreviousBeacon TCP](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/listeners/beacon-tcp)
[NextAgents](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/agents)

Last updated 2 days ago

Copy

    # CA cert
    openssl genrsa -out ca.key 2048
    openssl req -x509 -new -nodes -key ca.key -sha256 -days 3650 -out ca.crt -subj "/CN=Test CA"
    
    # server cert and key
    openssl genrsa -out server.key 2048
    openssl req -new -key server.key -out server.csr -subj "/CN=localhost"
    openssl x509 -req -in server.csr -CA ca.crt -CAkey ca.key -CAcreateserial -out server.crt -days 365 -sha256
    
    # client cert and key
    openssl genrsa -out client.key 2048
    openssl req -new -key client.key -out client.csr -subj "/CN=client"
    openssl x509 -req -in client.csr -CA ca.crt -CAkey ca.key -CAcreateserial -out client.crt -days 365 -sha256

---

# Beacon HTTP | Adaptix Framework

"Beacon HTTP" listener starts a web server and registers a "beacon" agent.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FKBgYb0ZcxNehR4ACjlMk%252FScreenshot_20251229_201021.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D913e6aa2-8f8a-4774-914a-f10c5e95c816&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=58fa4480&sv=2)

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/listeners/beacon-http#beacon-http-parameters)

Beacon HTTP parameters


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Main settings

HTTP Headers

Page Error

Page Payload

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FvzpDX5TgqRiTzX3nypPy%252FScreenshot_20250926_195225.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D99230a63-ef95-4588-b492-ee6a8806a23a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3aa62773&sv=2)

Parameter

Description

**Host & port (Bind)**

**Required.** The interface address and port to which your HTTP Beacon web server will bind.

**Callback addresses**

**Required.** List of address:port to which the agent will send requests. Current server rotation strategy: round-robin.

**Method**

The HTTP method that the agent will use to transmit data to the server and receive commands

**URI**

**Required.** The HTTP endpoint to which the agent sends the request.

**User-Agent**

**Required.** User-Agent for HTTP requests

**Heartbeat Header**

**Required.** The HTTP header in which the agent will transmit registration information

**Encryption key**

**Required.** Communication channel encryption key

**Use SSL**

If set, use HTTPS. If the SSL certificate and key are not specified, the server will generate them itself.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FgYhRwj6oKG4g6WITCVrs%252F62.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0d791382-bf02-49ce-80e4-0cf23fe518ad&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7e8139c5&sv=2)

Parameter

Description

**Trust X-Forwarded-For**

This option decides if listener uses the X-Forwarded-For HTTP header to determine the remote address of a request. _Use this option if your AdaptixServer is behind an HTTP redirector_

**Host Header**

Host header for HTTP requests

Request Headers

HTTP headers that the agent will use when sending the request

Server Headers

HTTP headers that will be in the server's response.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FeVbZfzYXsChu4iO3trjf%252F63.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D44eafd84-5600-4c67-8587-e3f924fd207b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c6cbc34a&sv=2)

**Page Error** \- the HTTP server's response to any request that is not from an agent.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FeWPgrao8RT0zK0o32IK6%252F64.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dda968bf3-2068-463d-b872-0248214d27fb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1510685&sv=2)

**Page Payload** - Server response to agent request. `<<<PAYLOAD_DATA>>>` will be replaced with data for the agent.

[PreviousListeners](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/listeners)
[NextBeacon SMB](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/listeners/beacon-smb)

# Beacon BOFs | Adaptix Framework

**AX BOF APIs:**

Copy

    void AxAddScreenshot(char* note, char* data, int len);
    void AxDownloadMemory(char* filename, char* data, int len);

**Beacon currently supports the following BOF APIs:**

Copy

    // Data Parser API
    char* BeaconDataExtract (datap * parser, int * size)
    int BeaconDataInt (datap * parser)
    int BeaconDataLength (datap * parser)
    void BeaconDataParse (datap * parser, char * buffer, int size)
    short BeaconDataShort (datap * parser)
    
    // Output API
    void BeaconPrintf (int type, char * fmt, ...)
    void BeaconOutput (int type, char * data, int len)
    
    //  Format API
    void BeaconFormatAlloc (formatp * obj, int maxsz)
    void BeaconFormatAppend (formatp * obj, char * data, int len)
    void BeaconFormatFree (formatp * obj)
    void BeaconFormatInt (formatp * obj, int val)
    void BeaconFormatPrintf (formatp * obj, char * fmt, ...)
    void BeaconFormatReset (formatp * obj)
    char* BeaconFormatToString (formatp * obj, int * size)
    
    // Internal APIs
    BOOL BeaconUseToken (HANDLE token)
    void BeaconRevertToken ()
    BOOL BeaconIsAdmIn ()
    BOOL toWideChar (char * src, wchar_t * dst, int max)
    
    BOOL BeaconAddValue (const char * key, void * ptr);
    void * BeaconGetValue (const char * key);
    BOOL BeaconRemoveValue (const char * key);

**Unsupported BOF APIs:**

[PreviousBeacon](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/agents/beacon)
[NextGopher](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/agents/gopher)

    LPVOID BeaconVirtualAllocEx(HANDLE processHandle, LPVOID lpAddress, SIZE_T dwSize, DWORD flAllocationType, DWORD flProtect);
    BOOL BeaconVirtualProtect(LPVOID lpAddress, SIZE_T dwSize, DWORD flNewProtect, PDWORD lpflOldProtect);
    BOOL BeaconVirtualProtectEx(HANDLE processHandle, LPVOID lpAddress, SIZE_T dwSize, DWORD flNewProtect, PDWORD lpflOldProtect);
    BOOL BeaconVirtualFree(LPVOID lpAddress, SIZE_T dwSize, DWORD dwFreeType);
    BOOL BeaconGetThreadContext(HANDLE threadHandle, PCONTEXT threadContext);
    BOOL BeaconSetThreadContext(HANDLE threadHandle, PCONTEXT threadContext);
    DWORD BeaconResumeThread(HANDLE threadHandle);
    HANDLE BeaconOpenProcess(DWORD desiredAccess, BOOL inheritHandle, DWORD processId);
    HANDLE BeaconOpenThread(DWORD desiredAccess, BOOL inheritHandle, DWORD threadId);
    BOOL BeaconCloseHandle(HANDLE object);
    BOOL BeaconUnmapViewOfFile(LPCVOID baseAddress);
    SIZE_T BeaconVirtualQuery(LPCVOID address, PMEMORY_BASIC_INFORMATION buffer, SIZE_T length);
    BOOL BeaconDuplicateHandle(HANDLE hSourceProcessHandle, HANDLE hSourceHandle, HANDLE hTargetProcessHandle, LPHANDLE lpTargetHandle, DWORD dwDesiredAccess, BOOL bInheritHandle, DWORD dwOptions);
    BOOL BeaconReadProcessMemory(HANDLE hProcess, LPCVOID lpBaseAddress, LPVOID lpBuffer, SIZE_T nSize, SIZE_T *lpNumberOfBytesRead);
    BOOL BeaconWriteProcessMemory(HANDLE hProcess, LPVOID lpBaseAddress, LPCVOID lpBuffer, SIZE_T nSize, SIZE_T *lpNumberOfBytesWritten);
    VOID BeaconDisableBeaconGate();
    VOID BeaconEnableBeaconGate();

# Gopher | Adaptix Framework

This version of the Gopher agent is not designed for AV or EDR evasion and is therefore not OPSEC compliant. Gopher is primarily intended to test and demonstrate the capabilities of AdaptixC2. However, the Gopher agent can be easily extended and modified, making it compatible with various AV evasion methods.

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/agents/gopher#configuration)

Configuration


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FeJPOWU2ktiuoB9OgG3FX%252FScreenshot_20251229_200222.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc7d6f6ff-37ea-405d-8009-98194f0403fe&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fda9a747&sv=2)

Gopher currently **supports Windows, Linux and MacOS**. The Gopher can be generated **for amd64 and arm64** architectures.

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/agents/gopher#commands)

Commands


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Gopher currently supports the following commands.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FXCLqdNoKcTHTQOZQoKA5%252FScreenshot_20250427_215852.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5bce04f8-b6c4-4ca0-9f22-ca1f05aafb91&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e6a9db8e&sv=2)

The **download** and **run** commands create a new parallel connection. The **job kill** command can stop the download or execution of a command/script.

# BOF and Extensions | Adaptix Framework

Official extensions: [https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/Extension-Kit](https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/Extension-Kit)

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/bof-and-extensions#beacon-object-files)

Beacon Object Files


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

BOF is just a block of position-independent code that receives pointers to some Beacon internal APIs. BOFs are single-file C programs that call Win32 APIs and limited [Beacon APIs](https://hstechdocs.helpsystems.com/manuals/cobaltstrike/current/userguide/content/topics/beacon-object-files_bof-c-api.htm)
.

AdaptixC2 expects that your BOFs are single-threaded programs that run for a short period of time. BOFs will block other agent tasks and functionality from executing. BOFs execute inside of your agent. If a BOF crashes, you will lose access. Write your BOFs carefully.

### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/bof-and-extensions#description-of-bof-for-agents)

Description of BOF for agents

[Beacon BOFs](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/agents/beacon/beacon-bofs)
[Gopher BOFs](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/agents/gopher/gopher-bofs)

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/bof-and-extensions#extensions)

Extensions


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[How to execute AxScript](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/how-to-execute-axscript)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FPVXLw0sNpy9JDkze8fti%252FScreenshot_20250724_194751.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De164eeab-6183-4695-8145-d74a92fe22dc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fde902e0&sv=2)

The extension file is an AxScript that must start with a global definition of the metadata variable that has the following properties: .

*   `name` - extension name,
    
*   `description` - extension description
    
*   `store` - determines whether the extension should be stored in the database (default: `true`).
    

Typically, extensions register new commands to call already registered commands. An example of defining a `shell` command that calls the command `ps run -o ...`. [See more details here](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axcommand-type)
.

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/bof-and-extensions#axscript-and-bofs)

AxScript and BOFs


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You'll likely want to use AxScript to run your finalized BOF implementations within AdaptixC2. A BOF is a good place to implement a lateral movement technique, an escalation of privilege tool, or a new reconnaissance capability.

Each agent has its own command to execute BOF. For example, for a beacon agent it is `execute bof`. Here is a script to run a `screenshot_bof` BOF:

First, the script gets the `note` and `pid` values. The next step is to pack our arguments. The [bof\_pack](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction#bof_pack)
 function packs arguments in a way that is compatible with Beacon's internal data parser API. This script uses [execute\_alias](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axcommand-type/commands-and-hooks#execute_alias)
 to run BOF with its arguments.

[PreviousScreenshots Manager](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/data-management/screenshots-manager)
[NextTunnels and Forwarding](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/tunnels-and-forwarding)

Last updated 5 months ago

*   [Beacon Object Files](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/bof-and-extensions#beacon-object-files)
    
*   [Description of BOF for agents](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/bof-and-extensions#description-of-bof-for-agents)
    
*   [Extensions](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/bof-and-extensions#extensions)
    
*   [AxScript and BOFs](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/bof-and-extensions#axscript-and-bofs)
    

Copy

    var metadata = {
        name: "Elevation-BOF",
        description: "BOFs for context elevation",
        store: true
    };
    
    // AxScript code
    // ...

Copy

    let cmd_shell = ax.create_command("shell", "Execute command via cmd.exe", "shell whoami /all");
    cmd_shell.addArgString("cmd_params", true);
    cmd_shell.setPreHook(function (id, cmdline, parsed_json, ...parsed_lines) {
        let new_cmd = "ps run -o C:\\Windows\\System32\\cmd.exe /c " + parsed_json["cmd_params"];
        ax.execute_alias(id, cmdline, new_cmd);
    });
    

Copy

    var cmd_screenshot = ax.create_command("screenshot_bof", "Alternative screenshot capability that does not do fork n run by @codex_tf2", "screenshot -n screen1 -p 812");
    cmd_screenshot.addArgFlagString("-n", "note", "Screenshot caption", "ScreenshotBOF");
    cmd_screenshot.addArgFlagInt("-p", "pid", "PID of the application whose window screenshot will be taken. If 0, then a full-screen screenshot", 0);
    cmd_screenshot.setPreHook(function (id, cmdline, parsed_json, ...parsed_lines) {
        let note = parsed_json["note"];
        let pid  = parsed_json["pid"];
    
        let bof_params = ax.bof_pack("cstr,int", [note, pid]);
        let bof_path = ax.script_dir() + "_bin/Screenshot." + ax.arch(id) + ".o";
    
        ax.execute_alias(id, cmdline, `execute bof ${bof_path} ${bof_params}`, "Task: Screenshot BOF");
    });

# Version 1.0 | Adaptix Framework

The client and server database structures have been changed and are not backward compatible with previous versions.

Contributors to the GitHub update include: [shashinma](https://github.com/shashinma)
, [P0142](https://github.com/P0142)
, [bri5ee](https://github.com/bri5ee)
, [BlackMeerkat](https://github.com/BlackMeerkat)

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/version-1.0#adaptixc2)

AdaptixC2


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   Network tunnels SOCKS4/SOCKS5 have been completely reworked on both client and server sides, significantly improving stability, performance, and speed. Tunnels are now RFC-compliant, which allows port scanning through tunnels. SOCKS5 tunnels (both client-side and server-side) now support IPv6 (Client and TeamServer). Added an internal TeamServer API for service responses to the SOCKS client about connection status: `TsTunnelConnectionHalt(channelId int, errorCode byte)`
    
*   The session graph has been completely redesigned. New icons have been added. Support for Top-Bottom layout has been introduced. Sessions through which tunnels are operating are now marked as TunS (tunnel via TeamServer) and TunC (tunnel via client). Inactive and Terminated sessions are no longer displayed on the graph. Quick session console opening via mouse middle-click.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FP9DKARFpkY5yaF4TKWx8%252FScreenshot_20251229_225406.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D44c8175b-cf3e-4d76-a08f-48fd4facf203&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1480ac6c&sv=2)

*   Dialog windows have been reworked and a profile system with background saving to the client database has been added for: Authorization Form, Listener Creation Window, Agent Generation Window. The authorization form now requires specifying a project directory, which will be used as the base path for all file system dialogs.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F48XLkIdBfPj28Pj3QSlB%252FScreenshot_20251229_204213.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daac4f74e-8139-4ae9-b3a3-94e19847be63&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3f7b51e7&sv=2)

*   Implemented Remote Shell — an interactive Non-PTY shell. This required rewriting the API `TsTerminalConnResume(agentId, terminalId, ioDirect bool)`.
    
*   Remote Terminal now operates in SSH-like mode (fast input + stable PTY). Multiple terminals can now be created within a single Remote Terminal tab.
    

Term 1

Term2

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fegld7ifphDuWDNAbzz5p%252FScreenshot_20251229_220225.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D05295ca9-49b1-48a7-bc90-18bc29e56f6d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=81691a1b&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FaDsFMwPvMVjgbooZYWUv%252FScreenshot_20251229_220230.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc816268f-a3e3-44fb-bcb4-a8f9a42af3ff&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b458afd9&sv=2)

*   The client now interacts with the server using asynchronous functions
    
*   AxScript is now executed asynchronously if the script does not use UI elements
    
*   A Handler mechanism for commands executed via AxScript has been implemented using new Ax APIs: [execute\_alias](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axcommand-type/commands-and-hooks#execute_alias)
    , [execute\_alias\_hook](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axcommand-type/commands-and-hooks#execute_alias)
    , [execute\_alias\_handler](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axcommand-type/commands-and-hooks#execute_alias)
    , [execute\_command](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axcommand-type/commands-and-hooks#execute_command)
    , [execute\_command\_hook](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axcommand-type/commands-and-hooks#execute_command)
    , [execute\_command\_handler](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axcommand-type/commands-and-hooks#execute_command)
    
*   When a command is entered incorrectly, the help output is now displayed by default.
    
*   Added the ability to modify session parameters via the context menu
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FKVqsae4dOJ19np9J9gkP%252FScreenshot_20251229_223727.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De5ab1deb-3fb4-49b9-9304-06868b1eb380&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=77b7fa49&sv=2)

*   Added tab blinking animation for background updates (by [shashinma](https://github.com/shashinma))
    )
    
*   Added the ability to rename tabs via the context menu (by [shashinma](https://github.com/shashinma))
    )
    
*   Tabs can now be closed by middle-clicking the tab or using a three-finger touchpad gesture
    
*   Added text batching to prevent UI freezes: flush every 100 ms or 64 KB, optimized bulk line removal, and added a database truncation limit of 10 MB (by [bri5ee](https://github.com/bri5ee)
    )
    
*   The Listener Manager now includes a Created column with the listener creation date and time
    
*   The Sessions table now includes a Created column with the agent creation date and time
    
*   Targets Manager now supports copying data to the clipboard
    
*   Credentials Manager now supports copying data to the clipboard. When copying credentials, templates can now be selected (impacket, netexec, etc.)
    
*   DownloadsManager now allows deleting multiple saved files at once
    
*   In all tables, Ctrl+F now enables filtering and searching. The search field supports conditional operators: `and` &, `or` |, `not` ^, `grouping` ().
    
*   The client synchronization system has been updated
    
*   Added new themes: Adaptix Dark and Adaptix Light
    

Ax Dark

# How to execute AxScript | Adaptix Framework

AxScript is built into the Adaptix client. To permanent load a script, go to **AxScript -> Script Manager** and select **Load new** from the context menu.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fw8Kbldn0OgYSwYfFCxb3%252FScreenshot_20250724_193520.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd37644ea-b2a3-4410-9094-9b483c8fb6db&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=eb8eb112&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FPVXLw0sNpy9JDkze8fti%252FScreenshot_20250724_194751.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De164eeab-6183-4695-8145-d74a92fe22dc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fde902e0&sv=2)

If your script fails to load, an error and tracelog will appear in the AxScript Console.

For testing scripts and programming, Adaptix Client provides AxScript Console.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FZBNHcKIGXJGOrekJU2F8%252FScreenshot_20250724_193625.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De7bedba9-4c03-4060-a1ce-3d65afce51bf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=eb6e5f07&sv=2)

AxScript displays output using `ax.log` functions.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F03v27mcp9z6pVekQdCYB%252FScreenshot_20250724_195224.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3df64696-292f-4f5c-b7f5-b2c739c5b09a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7823c75c&sv=2)

[PreviousAxScript](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript)
[NextIntroduction](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/introduction)

# AxScript | Adaptix Framework

AxScript is the scripting language built into AdaptixC2, version 0.7, and later. AxScript allows you to modify and extend the AdaptixClient to your needs. AxScript was designed with inspiration from Agressor Script, the scripting language behind Cobalt Strike.

[How to execute AxScript](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/how-to-execute-axscript)
[Introduction](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/introduction)
[AxFunction](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction)
[AxCommand type](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axcommand-type)
[AxForm type](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type)
[AxSelector type](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axselector-type)
[AxEvent type](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axevent-type)
[AxMenu type](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axmenu-type)

[PreviousGopher BOFs](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/agents/gopher/gopher-bofs)
[NextHow to execute AxScript](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/how-to-execute-axscript)

Last updated 5 months ago

# User Interface | Adaptix Framework

The AdaptixClient user interface is divided into two main parts. The Session Table, Session Graph, and Tasks Manager widgets are initially docked in the upper part. The lower part contains tabs for each function you interact with.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FOKYspOwQrc2jrNGCby4E%252FScreenshot_20251229_204430.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da7a3f02d-8018-4f6d-a965-d239b52f2fd0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a25e0015&sv=2)

Each widget can be moved around in its Dock, grouped into Tabs, or undocked as a separate window.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F1B6aWVVxDmiuEB3XrMrQ%252FScreenshot_20250927_213254.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dab0f5423-8d11-4bb3-97bd-c4eff8e478c1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7ebff42c&sv=2)

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/user-interface#main-menu)

Main menu


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/user-interface#id-1.-projects)

1\. Projects

Project Management Menu. Close Project will disconnect the current project from the C2 server and close the project area. New Project will open a new login window.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FbQ2xMOExLd1xUH0hKfqk%252FScreenshot_20250727_223654.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D74141687-8cad-4623-9eaa-2d4be49a3a80&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7b28ce9a&sv=2)

After authorization, a new project tab will appear in the bottom panel of the client.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FkRiMGIqwFPVoPpx6cbW3%252FScreenshot_20250224_205358.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db4d6f309-bdb9-47ab-a928-cb23e19e8d5b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e08a8065&sv=2)

### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/user-interface#id-2.-extender)

2\. Extender

Opens the extensions window for the client. More information about extensions [here](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/bof-and-extensions)
.

### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/user-interface#id-3.-settings)

3\. Settings

Opens the client settings window.

Main Settings

Sessions Table

Tasks table

Blinking tabs

Basic client settings: theme, fonts, session graph version and buffer size for [RemoteTerminal](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/agent-browsers/remote-terminal-shell)
.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fwbl96LWHZi4VRrHR6GfR%252FScreenshot_20251229_205004.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De52b9ac6-58d8-4c10-8260-c7a52e14f47a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9c8a053f&sv=2)

Agent Console block allows you to set the default buffer size, as well as the console time display modes, line feeds, and auto-scroll to the last output.

Allows you to select which fields will be displayed in the [Sessions Table.](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/user-interface#session-table)
 This section enables the HealthCheck feature and sets the agent monitoring time.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FcjBDU0E24ZW5hSonMOGb%252FScreenshot_20251229_205008.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db6e75f6e-4f2c-4e71-b98a-872018a5e249&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=eff079dc&sv=2)

Allows you to select which fields will be displayed in the [TasksTable](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/data-management/tasks-manager)
.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FyepsoDBkH4a0kFlbZrxg%252FScreenshot_20251229_205012.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D57c774f2-0329-4728-ad92-5cc9f06c139b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=71670069&sv=2)

This section allows you to select the docks that will highlight content changes.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FI7h41A2M4d9M8LRy0HDd%252FScreenshot_20251229_205016.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D866cc293-3531-41f1-9ee3-e53b0b01d92f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ed532182&sv=2)

Toolbar


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The toolbar at the top of AdaptixClient offers quick access to common Adaptix functions.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F0YdBkTjZrBogIUfjc03L%252F11.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5952fc52-57db-4602-8bb5-575e439d4d47&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fecea9a5&sv=2)

Manage listeners. Generate agents.

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/user-interface#session-table)

Session Table


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The session table shows which agents have registered with the AdaptixServer.

The User field displays the access token used. The session table has agent markings: _Terminated_, _Inactive_, _Unlink_, _No response_. The operator can mark an agent as _Inactive_ or _Active_, and also select the color of the entry or the entire line. The time for marking an agent as _No Response_ is set in the session table settings.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fs3BewxSFOD9B4ghXUUkq%252FScreenshot_20250427_121831.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbe718d6a-3e04-4fe3-aeb3-b6eb04e2cb9a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3a196218&sv=2)

Hovering over the Sleep field will show the current KillDate and WorkTime settings (if set). During non-working hours, the agent will be marked as "No worktime".

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fq6dnkHPxhUf2rNh1NSyi%252FScreenshot_20250427_222916.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddbab4ac0-e514-4156-a4d6-5d88615330f3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7ace57f6&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FM8r3q0I9enlktuGSnD2F%252FScreenshot_20250427_223011.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De17455c7-334a-423c-9dba-29643ce8cf44&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1e1e6a52&sv=2)

Double-clicking on an agent line will open the agent console. Agents are managed via the context menu of the session table.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FkMK2ih6Wg71etkxGjnPH%252FScreenshot_20251229_223630.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db261a66f-a641-45a8-9240-4c59dbf89ace&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6c0cc1c2&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F7i7EeAq3n3KI7HbAVyJO%252FScreenshot_20251229_223652.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D91e1dbcb-c613-4f19-afad-265398a1560b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a0b4cc94&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FXar1ptvPW9UWNdnPjgkm%252FScreenshot_20251229_223703.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd8dac536-b57d-4001-b205-4473d6ab1547&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1eccf8c7&sv=2)

When deleting an agent from the server via the "Remove from server" menu item through the session table menu, you now need to confirm the action.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FcUNPLxBx40Z1nanVhSKe%252FScreenshot_20250327_163020.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df218c96d-088c-46ba-807f-124fcec26656&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c28ea2b7&sv=2)

"**Set data**" allows you to manually set session data.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FfXQJQJ3gvWJ8xH773i0B%252FScreenshot_20251229_223727.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dace6080a-464f-4251-82b3-f5addf696756&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=27926da9&sv=2)

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/user-interface#search-and-filter)

Search and filter


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

All tables support searching and filtering data. To display the search and filter bar, use the keyboard shortcut `Ctrl+F`.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fdv3VHgomg9rz3Jwhl4re%252FScreenshot_20251229_224113.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3e505db3-928a-49ae-ac01-d41cc0bf89d5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=89c6833b&sv=2)

The search field supports groupings and conditions:

*   `()` - group
    
*   `^()` - not
    
*   `|` - or
    
*   `&` - and.
    

If **auto** check is active, searching and filtering are performed online whenever the filter is changed. If **auto** check is disabled, searching and filtering are performed only by pressing Enter.

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/user-interface#sessions-graph)

Sessions Graph


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Without a visual representation, it’s difficult to track and understand chains of 4 or 5 linked agents. That’s where the Sessions Graph comes in handy.

The session graph shows the agent chains in a natural way. Each agent session has a computer icon that indicates its operating system and privilege level. If the icon is red, the agent is running in a privileged process. A gray icon indicates that the agent is currently checked (possibly inactive).

The firewall icon represents the egress point of your agent. Each line contains the name of the listener responsible for processing agent data. A **dashed green line** indicates the use of "external" listeners.

A **solid yellow line** connecting one agent session to another represents a link between two agent ("internal" listener). These lines contain the listener name and the link name (e.g. `p0`).

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F51vghvWxFWRiZG4nKbTQ%252FScreenshot_20251229_211531.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc436e448-6ee4-44a8-b8b3-021eadd4c5ad&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=73d013f6&sv=2)

Agents are managed via the context menu of the session table.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F05hAFg4FLB36jjgFE5T5%252FScreenshot_20251229_224834.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0b3da2bb-0737-4fda-9bab-6439467e9190&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=72c1df51&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FCF1bFA9sqz3RgKhCw1nG%252FScreenshot_20251229_224844.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfc609c1b-d178-4420-8a0f-ebd8597f0dbf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=630dc515&sv=2)

If a network tunnel is running through the agent, this will be shown in the graph.

*   TunS - teamserver-side
    
*   TunC - client-side
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FqMw3IC2f8bnnVrmi0WbZ%252FScreenshot_20251229_225406.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db91ca2e3-ed80-4e09-86e7-0c0c7711f311&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=12e4ec01&sv=2)

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/user-interface#agents-console)

Agents console


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The agent console looks like this. Each command includes the operator name, task ID, and agent type.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fb5BEaXQNuR6zGpsQoi6m%252F20.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D362d02c6-1858-440e-92b4-fa94abe6e16f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5f41deef&sv=2)

The console keeps a history of entered commands, as well as autocompletion of commands. The console supports auto-completion of local paths by pressing the `Tab` key, and `Ctrl+Tab` will open a file selection window. The console has its own menu with many settings.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FoAIfJtQTbL2ZLy8tFsYM%252FScreenshot_20250624_002120.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D58775a7b-a57e-402d-b2b0-110d789bc5be&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ed751219&sv=2)

You can disable the display of time in the console in the application settings.

The console supports escaping quotes and slashes. An expression within the first quotation marks will be interpreted as a string for the console. If quotation marks need to be passed to a command, they must be escaped. An example of running mimikatz is below.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FRqT0DaVTszlNqQzyifrO%252FScreenshot_20251116_115807.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D31c14803-ed01-4878-b364-37df6bb02771&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d85b8ed8&sv=2)

# Introduction | Adaptix Framework

AxScript is built on top of the JavaScript engine from Qt's JSEngine framework. AxScript shares the same syntax as JavaScript:

*   variable definition and basic operations
    

Copy

    let a = 5 + 23;  // let - block environment
    if (a > 12) {
        var b = 12;  // var - global (func) environment
    }
    ax.log(b)        // print: 12

*   Basic String operations
    

Copy

    // Create
    let str1 = "Hello";
    let str2 = 'World';
    let str3 = `Hello ${str2}`;     // Hello World
    
    // Operations
    "Hello" + " " + "World"	        // "Hello World"
    "Hello".length	                // 5
    "Hello"[1]	                // "e"
    "Hello".includes("ell")	        // true
    "Hello".replace("llo", "y")	// "Hey"
    "a,b,c".split(",")	        // ["a", "b", "c"]
    "Hello".slice(1, 3)	        // "el"
    "Hello".toUpperCase()	        // "HELLO"
    
    // ... And other string JS operations

*   Basic Array operations
    

*   Basic Map/Object operations
    

*   Function Declaration
    

*   Functions and parameters
    

*   You can interrupt the execution of a function or script and pass the error to the underlying client using `throw`.
    

*   Regular Expressions
    

This is a small and incomplete example of what AxScript can do. For more information, see the Javascript reference.

[PreviousHow to execute AxScript](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/how-to-execute-axscript)
[NextAxFunction](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction)

Last updated 5 months ago

Copy

    // Create
    let arr1 = [1, 2, 3];
    let arr2 = new Array(1, 2, 3);
    let arr3 = ["a", 42, true, { name: "John" }];
    
    // Operations
    arr1.length                 // 3
    arr1[1]	                    // 20
    arr1.push(10)	            // 4 (arr1: [1, 2, 3, 10])
    arr1.pop()                  // 3 (arr1: [1, 2])
    arr1.unshift(10)            // 4 [10, 1, 2, 3]
    arr1.shift()                // 1 (arr1: [2, 3])
    arr1.concat([4, 5])         // [1, 2, 3, 4, 5]
    arr1.indexOf(2)             // 1
    arr1.includes(2)	    // true
    arr1.filter(x => x > 1)     // [2, 3]
    arr1.map(x => x * 2)	    // [2, 4, 6]
    [3, 1, 2].sort()	    // [1, 2, 3]
    [1, 2, 3].reverse()	    // [3, 2, 1]
    [1, 2, 3, 4].slice(1, 3)    // [2, 3]
    arr1.splice(1, 1, 99)       // [2] (arr1: [1, 99, 3])
    
    // ... And other array JS operations

Copy

    // Create
    let obj1 = { name: "Alice", age: 25 };
    let obj2 = new Object();
    obj2.key = "value";
    
    // Operations
    obj1.name	                         // "Alice"
    obj1["name"]	                         // "Alice"
    obj1.city = "Tokyo"	                 // { name: "Alice", age: 25, city: "Tokyo" }
    delete obj1.age	                         // { name: "Alice" }
    "name" in obj1	                         // true
    Object.keys(obj1)	                 // ["name", "age"]
    Object.values(obj1)	                 // ["Alice", 25]
    let newObj = { ...obj1 }	         // copy of
    Object.assign({}, obj1, { city: "Tokyo" })  // {name: "Alice", age: 25, city: "Tokyo"}
    
    // ... And other object JS operations

Copy

    // Classic
    function greet(name) {
      return `Hello, ${name}!`;
    }
    ax.log(greet("Alice")); // "Hello, Alice!"
    
    
    // Expression
    const greet = function(name) {
      return `Hello, ${name}!`;
    };
    ax.log(greet("Bob")); // "Hello, Bob!"
    
    
    // Arrow
    const greet = (name) => `Hello, ${name}!`;
    ax.log(greet("Charlie")); // "Hello, Charlie!"

Copy

    // Default
    function greet(name = "Guest") {
      return `Hello, ${name}!`;
    }
    ax.log(greet()); // "Hello, Guest!"
    
    
    // Undefined number of arguments
    function greet(greeting, ...names) {
      return `${greeting}, ${names.join(", ")}!`;
    }
    ax.log(greet("Hello", "Alice", "Bob", "Charlie"));  // "Hello, Alice, Bob, Charlie!"
    
    
    // Arguments via object
    function greet({ name, age }) {
      return `${name} is ${age} years old.`;
    }
    ax.log(greet({ name: "Alice", age: 25 })); // "Alice is 25 years old."
    

Copy

    throw new Error("error text");

Copy

    /\d+/.test("123");                                // true
    "abcdef".match(/abc/);                            // abc
    "hello123".replace(/\d+/, "");                    // hello
    "one, two, three".split(/\s*,\s*/);               // ["one", "two", "three"]
    
    let regex = /hello/gi;
    "Hello HELLO hello".match(regex);                 // ["Hello", "HELLO", "hello"]
    
    let result = "2025-07-24".match(/(\d{4})-(\d{2})-(\d{2})/);
    result[1];     // 2025
    result[2];     // 07
    result[3];     // 24

---

# Beacon | Adaptix Framework

This version of the Beacon agent is not designed for AV or EDR evasion and is therefore not OPSEC compliant. Beacon is primarily intended to test and demonstrate the capabilities of AdaptixC2. However, the Beacon agent can be easily extended and modified, making it compatible with various AV evasion methods.

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/agents/beacon#configuration)

Configuration


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

EXE

SHELLCODE

DLL

SERVICE

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FjxTGRFgc8UyuX2gQdRCN%252FScreenshot_20251229_200158.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D19bfe6e0-d670-4444-861f-a82c5d11d45c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f0431793&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FygekCepvUnQOjQHilWW0%252FScreenshot_20251229_200204.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D15f9d282-be19-4987-89c2-4dfb0f68a230&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=36cecb2c&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FLyBnwApLA2IpxHrMgJF3%252FScreenshot_20251229_200207.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0180955c-8bc1-4206-97ab-1c1f0195583d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f7d27e4c&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F2eBXlV5MqDCLWXkgyqLe%252FScreenshot_20251229_200211.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D56feb83e-313d-4951-ad92-674bbcbe1a2b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=694ee913&sv=2)

Beacon currently **only supports Windows OS**.

The Beacon can be generated **for x64 and x86** architectures in the following formats: EXE, DLL, Service Executable, Shellcode.

The **KillDate** parameter sets the date and time of the beacon's death (GMT+0 format).

The **WorkingTime** parameter sets the time interval during which the beacon will be active (local time on the target host).

*   The **Service Name** is set for the Service Executable.
    
*   The **Legit-DLL** is set for the DLL. This option will generate a DLL for Sideloading that will contain all exports from the specified DLL.
    

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/agents/beacon#commands)

Tunnel commands

Command

Description

socks start

Start a SOCKS4/5 proxy server (with/out auth) and listen on a specified port

socks stop

Stop a SOCKS proxy server

Start local port forwarding from server via agent

lportfwd stop

Stop local port forwarding

rportfwd start

Start remote port forwarding from agent via server

rportfwd stop

Stop remote port forwarding

Since Bacon is an asynchronous agent, proxy scanning should be performed with no more than four threads. Tested on NetExec SMB... Agent does not switch sleep time automatically. Use `sleep 0`

Agent command

Command

Description

sleep

Sets sleep time

terminate thread

Terminate the main beacon thread (without terminating the process)

terminate process

Terminate the beacon process

profile workingtime

Set the start and end time of the beacon activity. Time interval in the format 'HH:mm(start)-HH:mm(end)'. Set 0 to disable the option.

profile killdate

Set the date and time for the beacon to stop working. Datetime 'DD.MM.YYYY hh:mm:ss' in **GMT format**. Set 0 to disable the option
