Table


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `table` elements provides an item-based table view.

`element create_table(string[] headers)` - Creates a new `table` view with the given headers.

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#methods-12)

Methods:

1

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#addcolumn)

addColumn

This method adds a new column to the table with the specified `header`.

2

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#setcolumns)

setColumns

This method adds new columns to the table with the specified `headers`.

3

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#additem-2)

addItem

Inserts `item` at the end of the table, `item` is an array of strings, the string index corresponds to the column index.

4

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#rowcount)

rowCount

Returns the number of rows.

5

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#columncount)

columnCount

Returns the number of columns.

6

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#text-3)

text

This property contains the cell text for the specified `row` and `column`. If no text is specified, an empty string is returned.

7

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#setitemtext-1)

setItemText

Set the cell text for the specified `row` and `column`.

8

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#clear-2)

clear

Removes all items from table.

9

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#setrowcount)

setRowCount

Sets the number of `rows` in this `table`'s.

10

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#setcolumncount)

setColumnCount

Sets the number of `cols` in this `table`'s.

11

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#currentrow-1)

currentRow

This method return the row of the current cell.

12

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#currentcolumn)

currentColumn

This method return the column of the current cell.

13

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#hidecolumn)

hideColumn

Hide the given `column`.

14

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#selectedrows-1)

selectedRows

Returns an array of arrays of the selected elements.

15

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#setreadonly-3)

setReadOnly

This method holds whether the `table` is read-only.

16

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#setsortingenabled)

setSortingEnabled

If _enable_ is true, enables sorting for the table

17

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#resizetocontent)

resizeToContent

Will automatically resize the section to its optimal size based on the contents of the entire `column`.

18

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#setheadersvisible)

setHeadersVisible

If `enable` is true, the column in the table will be visible, otherwise hidden.

19

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#setcolumnalign)

setColumnAlign

Sets the alignment in the `column`. Available values are "left", "right", "center".

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#signals-6)

Signals:

1

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#cellchanged)

cellChanged

This signal is emitted whenever the data of the item in the cell specified by `row` and `column` has changed.

2

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#cellclicked)

cellClicked

This signal is emitted whenever a cell in the table is clicked. The `row` and `column` specified is the cell that was clicked.

3

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#celldoubleclicked)

cellDoubleClicked

This signal is emitted whenever a cell in the table is double clicked. The `row` and `column` specified is the cell that was double clicked.

Example[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#example-16)

GroupBox


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `groupbox` element provides a group box frame with a title.

`element create_groupbox(string title, bool checkable)` - Constructs a `groupbox` with the given `title`. Property `checkable` holds whether the group box has a checkbox in its title.

isCheckable

If this property is `true`, the group box displays its title using a checkbox in place of an ordinary label.

4

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#setcheckable)

setCheckable

If `checkable` is `true`, the group box displays its title using a checkbox in place of an ordinary label.

Stack


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `stack` element provides a stack of widgets where only one widget is visible at a time.

`element create_stack()` - Constructs a `stack`.

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#methods-18)

Methods:

1

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#addpage-1)

addPage

2

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#insertpage)

insertPage

Inserts the given `page` at the given `index` in the `stack`.

3

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#removepage)

removePage

Removes element from the `stack` by `index`.

4

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#setcurrentindex-1)

setCurrentIndex

This method set the `index` position of the widget that is visible;

5

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#currentindex-1)

currentIndex

This method return the `index` position of the widget that is visible;

6

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#count-1)

count

This method return the number of elements contained by this `stack`.

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#signals-9)

Signals:

1

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#currentchanged)

currentChanged

This signal is emitted whenever the current element changes.

Example[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#example-22)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FkpSwggVHQkbNiTZ9KIxL%252FScreenshot_20250726_012107.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd265f63e-435c-488d-bb6e-88f8fbfb6f97&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=40f39975&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#dialog)

Dialog


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `dialog` element is implement of dialog windows.

`dialog create_dialog(string title)` - Constructs a `dialog` with `title`.

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#methods-19)

Methods:

1

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#setbuttonstext)

setButtonsText

This method sets the text `ok_text` for button OK and the text `cancel_text` for button CANCEL.

2

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#setsize)

setSize

This method sets the size for the window.

3

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#setlayout-1)

setLayout

Sets the layout manager for this window.

4

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#close)

close

Close window.

5

#### 

[](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#exec)

exec

Shows the dialog as a modal dialog, blocking until the user closes it. If the window is closed by pressing the OK button, the method will return true.

    void container::put(string id, element elem);

    string container::toJson();

Copy

    void container::fromJson(string jsonString);

Copy

    let tl1 = form.create_textline();
    let tl2 = form.create_textline();
    let tm3 = form.create_textmulti();
    let btn = form.create_button("Get data");
    
    let container = form.create_container()
    container.put("line1", tl1)
    container.put("lin2", tl2)
    
    form.connect(btn, "clicked", function(){
        tm3.setText(container.toJson());
    });
    
    let layout = form.create_vlayout();
    layout.addWidget(tl1);
    layout.addWidget(tl2);
    layout.addWidget(tm3);
    layout.addWidget(btn);
    
    let dialog = form.create_dialog("");
    dialog.setLayout(layout);
    dialog.exec()

    c1.setItems(["Item 1", "Item 2", "Item 3"]);
    
    let tl2 = form.create_textline();
    tl2.setReadOnly(true);

    stateChanged();

Copy

    let c1 = form.create_check("Checkbox");
    
    let tl2 = form.create_textline();
    tl2.setReadOnly(true);
    
    form.connect(c1, "stateChanged", function(){
        if(c1.isChecked())
            tl2.setText("Checked");
        else
            tl2.setText("UnChecked");
    });
    
    let layout = form.create_vlayout();
    layout.addWidget(c1);
    layout.addWidget(tl2);
    
    let dialog = form.create_dialog("");
    dialog.setLayout(layout);
    dialog.exec()

    let listw = form.create_list();
    listw.addItems(["Item 1", "Item 2", "Item 3"]);
    listw.addItem("New");
    
    let text_line   = form.create_textline(listw.count())
    let text_button = form.create_button("go");
    
    form.connect(text_button, "clicked", function (){
        text_line.setText(listw.items());
    })
    
    form.connect(listw, "itemClicked", function (text){
        text_line.setText(text);
    })
    
    let layout = form.create_gridlayout();
    layout.addWidget(listw,     0, 0, 1, 2);
    layout.addWidget(text_line, 1, 0, 1, 1);
    layout.addWidget(text_button, 1, 1, 1, 1);
    
    let dialog = form.create_dialog("");
    dialog.setSize(460, 240);
    dialog.setLayout(layout);
    dialog.exec()

Copy

    let table = form.create_table(["Name", "Age", "Id"])
    table.addItem(["Alex", "23", "a1a2"]);
    table.addItem(["Bella", "37", "b1c8"]);
    table.setColumnAlign(1, "center");
    
    let text_line   = form.create_textline(table.columnCount())
    let text_button = form.create_button("go");
    
    form.connect(text_button, "clicked", function (){
        text_line.setText(table.selectedRows());
    })
    
    form.connect(table, "cellChanged", function (row, column){
        text_line.setText(table.text(row, column));
    })
    
    let layout = form.create_gridlayout();
    layout.addWidget(table,     0, 0, 1, 2);
    layout.addWidget(text_line, 1, 0, 1, 1);
    layout.addWidget(text_button, 1, 1, 1, 1);
    
    let dialog = form.create_dialog("");
    dialog.setSize(460, 240);
    dialog.setLayout(layout);
    dialog.exec()

    let text_multi1 = form.create_textmulti("Panel 1");

    layout1.addWidget(combo_w,     1, 0, 1, 1);

    clicked(bool checked = false);

Copy

    let text_multi1 = form.create_textmulti("Panel 1");
    let combo_w = form.create_combo();
    combo_w.setItems(["Panel 1", "Panel 2"]);
    
    let layout1 = form.create_gridlayout();
    layout1.addWidget(text_multi1, 0, 0, 1, 1);
    layout1.addWidget(combo_w,     1, 0, 1, 1);
    
    let panel = form.create_panel();
    panel.setLayout(layout1);
    
    let group_box = form.create_groupbox("Box", true);
    group_box.setPanel(panel);
    
    form.connect(group_box, "clicked", function (checked){
        panel.setEnabled(checked);
    })
    
    let layout = form.create_gridlayout();
    layout.addWidget(group_box, 0, 0, 1, 1);
    
    let dialog = form.create_dialog("");
    dialog.setSize(460, 240);
    dialog.setLayout(layout);
    dialog.exec()

    void scrollarea::setWidgetResizable(bool resizable);

    void scrollarea::setPanel(element panel);

Copy

    let text_multi1 = form.create_textmulti("Panel 1");
    let text_multi2 = form.create_textmulti("Panel 2");
    let combo_w = form.create_combo();
    combo_w.setItems(["Panel 1", "Panel 2"]);
    
    
    let layout1 = form.create_gridlayout();
    layout1.addWidget(text_multi1, 0, 0, 1, 1);
    layout1.addWidget(text_multi2,     1, 0, 1, 1);
    layout1.addWidget(combo_w,     2, 0, 1, 1);
    
    let panel = form.create_panel();
    panel.setLayout(layout1);
    
    
    const scroll = form.create_scrollarea();
    scroll.setPanel(panel);
    
    let layout = form.create_gridlayout();
    layout.addWidget(scroll, 0, 0, 1, 1);
    
    let dialog = form.create_dialog("");
    dialog.setSize(460, 240);
    dialog.setLayout(layout);
    dialog.exec()

    let text_multi1 = form.create_textmulti("Panel 1");
    let text_multi2 = form.create_textmulti("Panel 2");
    
    let splitter = form.create_hsplitter();
    splitter.addPage(text_multi1);
    splitter.addPage(text_multi2);
    splitter.setSizes([100, 200]);
    
    let layout = form.create_gridlayout();
    layout.addWidget(splitter, 0, 0, 1, 1);

    dialog.setLayout(layout);

    currentChanged(int index);

Copy

    let text_multi1 = form.create_textmulti("Panel 1");
    let text_multi2 = form.create_textmulti("Panel 2");
    
    let stack_w = form.create_stack();
    stack_w.addPage(text_multi1);
    stack_w.addPage(text_multi2);
    
    let combo_w = form.create_combo();
    combo_w.setItems(["Panel 1", "Panel 2"]);
    
    form.connect(combo_w, "currentIndexChanged", function (index){
        stack_w.setCurrentIndex(index);
    })
    
    let layout = form.create_gridlayout();
    layout.addWidget(stack_w,   0, 0, 1, 1);
    layout.addWidget(combo_w, 1, 0, 1, 1);
    
    let dialog = form.create_dialog("");
    dialog.setSize(460, 240);
    dialog.setLayout(layout);
    dialog.exec()
